# Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings

## Overview

Four Skull Lookout

 This page lists the ancient **Nordic dwellings** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). This page only lists the smaller ruins, and the larger [Nordic ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") are listed on separate pages and use different map marker icons.

:    **[Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin south of Karthwasten containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Four+Skull+Lookout)
:    **[Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest")** — A small outdoor graveyard and Nordic ruin northwest of Whiterun containing skeletons and a draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hamvir%27s+Rest)
:    **[Journeyman's Nook](/wiki/Skyrim:Journeyman%27s_Nook "Skyrim:Journeyman's Nook")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin southeast of Winterhold containing a bandit. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Journeyman%27s+Nook)
:    **[Kjenstag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjenstag_Ruins "Skyrim:Kjenstag Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin east-northeast of Morthal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kjenstag+Ruins)
:    **[Lost Valkygg](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valkygg "Skyrim:Lost Valkygg")** — A small Nordic ruin northeast of Labyrinthian containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valkygg)
:    **[Moldering Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moldering_Ruins "Skyrim:Moldering Ruins")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small camp and concealed cave west of Rorikstead containing vampires and dead draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moldering+Ruins+%28DG%29)
:    **[North Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:North Skybound Watch")** — A small Nordic tower and ruin northeast of Helgen containing bandits and a giant frostbite spider. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skybound+Watch+Pass)
:    **[Roadside Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Roadside_Ruins "Skyrim:Roadside Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin northwest of Falkreath containing a spriggan. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Roadside+Ruins)
:    **[Skytemple Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Skytemple_Ruins "Skyrim:Skytemple Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin north of the College of Winterhold containing a draugr and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skytemple+Ruins)
:    **[Snowclad Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowclad_Ruins "Skyrim:Snowclad Ruins")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small outdoor Nordic ruin northwest of the Temple of Miraak containing werebears. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Snowclad+Ruins)
:    **[Windward Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Windward_Ruins "Skyrim:Windward Ruins")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin southwest of Dawnstar containing skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windward+Ruins)
:    **[Yorgrim Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Yorgrim_Overlook "Skyrim:Yorgrim Overlook")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin on the southern slope of the mountain range directly south of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yorgrim+Overlook)

# Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Learn about Nordic jewelry.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Automatically added after purchasing the [Nordic Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") |
| Location(s): | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") |
| Reward: | Ability to craft Nordic jewelry |
| ID: | ccEDHSSE001\_CraftsmanEncounterQuest |
| Added by: | [Nordic Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry") |

Two reavers have killed a master artisan

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Obtain a piece of Nordic jewelry and read the [*Certificate of Authenticity*](/wiki/Skyrim:Certificate_of_Authenticity "Skyrim:Certificate of Authenticity").
2. Travel to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") and locate [Hugin Ice-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Hugin_Ice-Shaper "Skyrim:Hugin Ice-Shaper") west of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
3. Read [*Hugin Ice-Shaper's Notebook*](/wiki/Skyrim:Hugin_Ice-Shaper%27s_Notebook "Skyrim:Hugin Ice-Shaper's Notebook") and craft an item of Nordic jewelry to complete the quest.

### Make a Purchase

Nordic circlet

Hugin Ice-Shaper

This quest will be added to your journal the first time you obtain a [Nordic Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Amulet "Skyrim:Nordic Amulet"), [Nordic Circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Circlet "Skyrim:Nordic Circlet"), or [Nordic Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ring "Skyrim:Nordic Ring"). A [*Certificate of Authenticity*](/wiki/Skyrim:Certificate_of_Authenticity "Skyrim:Certificate of Authenticity") will be automatically added to your inventory, and you will be directed to read it to progress the quest.

Nordic jewelry can be found in the world as random loot. Alternatively, all general goods and jewelry merchants will have these items available for sale, so the quickest method may be to purchase a piece from them. For example, in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") you can purchase Nordic jewelry from the [Pawned Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn") or from [Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi")'s stall in Riften Grand Plaza. Note that these items are all relatively pricey given that they're pieces of jewelry.

Once you've obtained your first piece of Nordic jewelry, read the certificate to learn that the creator of the jewelry is a craftsman named [Hugin Ice-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Hugin_Ice-Shaper "Skyrim:Hugin Ice-Shaper") who can be found on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

### Stalhrim Lapidary

Travel to Solstheim and you will be directed to a spot west of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), in the ash wastes just north of the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone"). There you will find two hostile [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") (a melee fighter and an archer) standing over the body of Hugin. Dispense with them both and loot the melee reaver for three powerful enchanted items: a leveled [Nordic Amulet of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Amulet_of_Health "Skyrim:Nordic Amulet of Health"), a leveled [Nordic Circlet of Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Circlet_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Nordic Circlet of Magicka"), and a leveled [Nordic Ring of Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ring_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Nordic Ring of Stamina"). You can then locate and read [*Hugin Ice-Shaper's Notebook*](/wiki/Skyrim:Hugin_Ice-Shaper%27s_Notebook "Skyrim:Hugin Ice-Shaper's Notebook") to learn how to craft Nordic jewelry.

To complete the quest, you will need to craft a piece of Nordic jewelry yourself. Be sure to grab the required components from the satchel next to the body: three samples of [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") and three [quicksilver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ingot "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ingot"). Head back into town and find a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") in order to craft the jewelry of your choice and finish the quest.

## Notes

- This quest was originally added to your journal automatically upon installing the [Nordic Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"). You would then be directed to Riften to purchase a Nordic jewelry item, although obtaining the jewelry via any other method would also progress the quest. This was changed with the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") update, and the quest now only starts once you have already obtained a Nordic jewelry item.
- The quest can also be started by simply approaching Hugin Ice-Shaper's corpse on Solstheim.

## Quest Stages

| Nordic Jewelry (ccEDHSSE001\_CraftsmanEncounterQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | I've heard traders are selling unique jewelry from Solstheim. I should see what they have to offer. *Objective 0:* Purchase a piece of Nordic Jewelry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Read the Certificate of Authenticity |
| 20 |  | This jewelry is made exclusively by a man named Hugin Ice-Shaper in Solstheim with rare stalhrim ore. Perhaps the craftsman has more items for sale. I should visit him in Raven Rock. *Objective 15:* Travel to Solstheim  *Objective 20:* Find the craftsman in Raven Rock |
| 30 |  | I have located the craftsman, but a pair of bandits seem to have found him first. I should search the area before anything of value is lost. |
| 30 |  | I stumbled on a bandit attack near Raven Rock. I should search the area before anything of value is lost. *Objective 40:* Inspect the area |
| 40 |  | *Objective 50:* Read Hugin Ice-Shaper's Notebook |
| 50 |  | Hugin Ice-Shaper met an untimely fate. I recovered his belongings before they could be looted by reavers. With what is left of his notes, perhaps I can continue his work. *Objective 60:* Craft a piece of Nordic Jewelry at a forge |
| 100 | ☑ | Using Hugin Ice-Shaper's notes, I learned to forge my own pieces of Nordic Jewelry. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 25, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccEDHSSE001_CraftsmanEncounterQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccEDHSSE001_CraftsmanEncounterQuest`.

# Skyrim:Nordic Ruins

## Overview

Concept art of Nordic Ruins

 This page lists all the **Nordic ruins** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:    **[Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Riften containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angarvunde)
:    **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin north of Riften containing draugr and necromancers led by Lu'ah Al-Skaven. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ansilvund)
:    **[Arcwind Point](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcwind_Point "Skyrim:Arcwind Point")** — A small outdoor Nordic ruin south of Ivarstead containing draugr, skeletons and, after Dragon Rising, a dragon. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arcwind+Point)
:    **[Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Riverwood containing bandits, draugr, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleak+Falls+Barrow)
:    **[Blind Cliff Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Bastion "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Bastion")** — A medium-sized cave southwest of Karthwasten along the banks of the Karth River containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
:    **[Bloodskal Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodskal_Barrow "Skyrim:Bloodskal Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin north of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bloodskal+Barrow)
:    **[Bromjunaar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bromjunaar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Bromjunaar Sanctuary")** — A hidden location reached by equipping the wooden mask while inside a building in Labyrinthian.
:    **[Champion's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Champion's Rest")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Umbra "Skyrim:Umbra") — A medium-sized Nordic ruin located in the Rift, east of Shor's Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Champion%27s+Rest+%28CC%29)
:    **[Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite")** — A small Nordic ruin southwest of Morthal containing draugr and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Men%27s+Respite)
:    **[Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt")** — A large Nordic ruin west of Dragon Bridge containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deepwood+Redoubt)
:    **[Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin northwest of Whiterun containing Silver Hands, draugr, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dustman%27s+Cairn)
:    **[Folgunthur](/wiki/Skyrim:Folgunthur "Skyrim:Folgunthur")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Solitude containing draugr, frostbite spiders, and the draugr Mikrul Gauldurson. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Folgunthur)
:    **[Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Riften containing Dragon Cultists, draugr, skeevers, and the dragon priest Rahgot. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forelhost)
:    **[Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin south-southwest of Dawnstar containing bandits and the unique wispmother the Pale Lady. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostmere+Crypt)
:    **[Geirmund's Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Skyrim:Geirmund's Hall")** — A small Nordic ruin east of Ivarstead containing draugr, frostbite spiders, skeevers, and the draugr Sigdis Gauldurson. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Geirmund%27s+Hall)
:    **[Gyldenhul Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin east of Skaal Village containing the spirit and treasure of Haknir Death-Brand. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Gyldenhul+Barrow)
:    **[Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt")** — A small Nordic ruin south of Markarth containing Forsworn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag+Rock+Redoubt)
:    **[Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End")** — A small Nordic ruin west of Dragon Bridge containing a hagraven, hags, and witches. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hag%27s+End)
:    **[High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Dawnstar containing draugr and the dragon priest Vokun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Gate+Ruins)
:    **[Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb")** — A small Nordic ruin southwest of Windhelm containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hillgrund%27s+Tomb)
:    **[Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow")** — A small Nordic ruin southwest of Winterhold containing draugr and the tomb of Warlord Gathrik. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironbind+Barrow)
:    **[Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins")** — A large ruined temple west of Solitude containing corrupted shades created by the necromancer Malkoran. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kilkreath+Ruins)
:    **[Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin southeast of Raven Rock containing draugr, spiders, and the dragon priest Ahzidal. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Kolbjorn+Barrow)
:    **[Korvanjund](/wiki/Skyrim:Korvanjund "Skyrim:Korvanjund")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin northeast of Whiterun containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Korvanjund)
:    **[Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian")** — A large Nordic ruin southeast of Morthal containing draugr, skeletons, trolls, wisps, and the dragon priest Morokei. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Labyrinthian)
:    **[Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt")** — A massive Nordic ruin inhabited by Forsworn and hagravens. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Valley+Redoubt)
:    **[Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin north of Markarth containing draugr and the dragon priest Otar the Mad. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ragnvald)
:    **[Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast")** — A small Nordic ruin east-northeast of Rorikstead containing subjugated ghosts and Sild the Warlock. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rannveig%27s+Fast)
:    **[Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southwest of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Saarthal)
:   **[Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze")** — A small Nordic ruin east of Labyrinthian containing atronachs and a dremora. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shalidor%27s+Maze)
:    **[Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion")** — A small Nordic ruin north of Falkreath containing vampires and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shriekwind+Bastion)
:    **[Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin east of Ivarstead containing draugr and skeletons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shroud+Hearth+Barrow)
:    **[Silent Moons Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Moons_Camp "Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp")** — A small Nordic ruin northwest of Whiterun containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Silent+Moons+Camp)
:    **[Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair")** — A small Nordic ruin south-southeast of Dawnstar containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Silverdrift+Lair)
:    **[Sivdur's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand") — A Nordic ruin located north of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sivdur%27s+Respite+%28CC%29)
:   **[Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn "Skyrim:Skuldafn")** — A large Nordic ruin with a portal to Sovngarde containing draugr, dragons, and a dragon priest. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Skuldafn)
:    **[Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin north-northeast of Windhelm containing draugr. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snow+Veil+Sanctum)
:    **[Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher")** — The location of the Pilgrim's Path and main entrance to Nocturnal's Ebonmere portal, resting place for the Skeleton Key. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Twilight+Sepulcher)
:    **[Ustengrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Ustengrav "Skyrim:Ustengrav")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin northeast of Morthal containing bandits, warlocks, draugr, skeletons, and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ustengrav)
:    **[Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Nordic ruin south-southeast of Thirsk Mead Hall containing corrupted shades, draugr, and the dragon priest Vahlok the Jailor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Vahlok%27s+Tomb)
:    **[Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Markarth containing draugr, frostbite spiders, skeevers, and the dragon priest Hevnoraak. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valthume)
:    **[Volskygge](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge "Skyrim:Volskygge")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin west of Solitude containing bandits, draugr, frostbite spiders, and the dragon priest Volsung. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Volskygge)
:    **[Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud")** — A medium-sized Nordic ruin southeast of Morthal containing draugr and the ghost of Kvenel the Tongue. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Volunruud)
:    **[White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A medium-sized Nordic ruin in the northern part of Solstheim inhabited by bandits and spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=White+Ridge+Barrow)
:    **[Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow")** — A small Nordic ruin northeast of Windhelm containing the shade of an ancient Nord warrior. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yngol+Barrow)
:    **[Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb")** — A small Nordic ruin northwest of Winterhold containing Companion ghosts, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ysgramor%27s+Tomb)

## Notes

- Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild")'s [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") map icon with the one used for Nordic ruins.

The Northern Maiden docked in Windhelm

The **Northern Maiden** is a ship initially docked at the [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") docks. It will dock at [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") after you buy passage to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

Ship docked in Raven Rock

# Skyrim:Northshore Landing

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Docks.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Docks.png) | Docks: Northshore Landing ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Northshore+Landing)) | | |

| Occupants | |
| [Mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab"), [Old Salty](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Salty "Skyrim:Old Salty") [Ancarion](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancarion "Skyrim:Ancarion"), [Thalmor Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Thalmor") | |

Northshore Landing

**Northshore Landing** is a small abandoned [dock](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Places#Docks "Skyrim:Other Places") on the northwest coast of [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim") inhabited by [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab").

Thalmor ship docked

It is west of [Castle Karstaag Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Ruins "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Ruins") and north-northeast of [Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave"). It stands in the shadow of the [Mortrag Glacier](/wiki/Lore:Mortrag_Glacier "Lore:Mortrag Glacier"), with a steep ice wall blocking land travel to the north.

## Related Quests

- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**: Find a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") missing from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").
- **[Sell Stalhrim Armor and Weapons to Ancarion](/wiki/Skyrim:Sell_Stalhrim_Armor_and_Weapons_to_Ancarion "Skyrim:Sell Stalhrim Armor and Weapons to Ancarion")**: Sell [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") equipment to [Ancarion](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancarion "Skyrim:Ancarion").

## Walkthrough

The dock itself consists of a T-shaped jetty, with the down leg pointing north and falling apart at the end. There are several [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") in and around the docks. On the jetty are five fish barrels, several crates, and four sacks, along with a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). The docks are by the mouth of a stream that is the runoff from a nearby waterfall in the mountains. A [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") is by the stream near the base of the waterfall, and behind the waterfall is an unlocked wooden chest. Along the shore and under the docks are several [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster"), [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam"), and stacks of crates, barrels, and chests. There is a partially flooded rowboat pulled up on shore to the west of the docks. On the hull is a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") cluster. On a crate to the immediate right of the stairs up to the docks is another barnacle cluster. Opposite the stairs, to the south, is a novice-locked chest. Due north of the rowboat, under the water, is an apprentice-locked chest beside a sunken boat with two Nordic barnacle clusters on the hull and a patch of [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") nearby. Under the docks, level with the end of the damaged jetty, are a couple crates with a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot") on the seabed between them.

On the east shore of the stream is an empty chest, with an [ebony ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Ebony Ore Vein") farther east against the cliffs, while to the north is a derelict shack with the doors and windows missing and holes in the roof and walls. The shack is home to a large, unique mudcrab, named [Old Salty](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Salty "Skyrim:Old Salty"). In front of the shack is an open box containing two pieces of [mudcrab chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin") beside two fish barrels, a food sack, and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). Inside, against the south wall, is a bookcase holding an expert-locked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") and many [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"). To the right of the bookcase is a bucket containing a piece of mudcrab chitin. Against the north wall are two fish barrels, an unlocked chest, and a long wooden table with a map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") on top. There are three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") placed over the capitals of three of the [holds](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds"), with a further thirteen loose septims, a [gold ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Ring"), and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") to the right, and a piece of mudcrab chitin to the left. If you look through the window at the table, there is also a [silver amethyst ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Amethyst_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Amethyst Ring") behind a crate that is difficult to see from inside.

If you come to Northshore Landing during the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim"), a large ship will be present at the dock. There will be a few [Thalmor soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Thalmor") standing guard or patrolling the area under the leadership of [Ancarion](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancarion "Skyrim:Ancarion").

## Notes

- A small [unmarked island](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Solstheim#Horker_Iceberg "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Solstheim") lies to the north, visible from Northshore Landing. There are two [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") deposits and a leveled enchanted [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") there guarded by two or three [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"). Once the stalhrim has been mined, one of the sarcophagi contains a dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") that can be looted.
- A novice-locked [random chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Another_Random_Chest "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") surrounded by riekling spears can be found to the southwest against the cliff face, near two horkers.
- During the quest, Old Salty and the rest of the mudcrabs won't be present once Ancarion and his men arrive at the dock. This is especially true if you convince them to become merchants for Stalhrim equipment.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map displays Northshore Landing without Ancarion's ship; the previous Solstheim satellite map displayed the area with the ship present.

## Bugs

- Followers may be unable to stay with you after visiting the island north of Northshore Landing due to the navmeshes not being connected properly.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.

Northwatch Keep

**Northwatch Keep** is a small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). It contains only one zone, *[Northwatch Keep](#Northwatch_Keep)*.

The fort is used as a jail by the Thalmor, and is off-limits to all others. Ignoring the warnings of the [Northwatch guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Guard "Skyrim:Northwatch Guard") at the entrance will result in the [patrolling guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor#Thalmor_Warriors "Skyrim:Thalmor") becoming hostile.

## Related Quests

- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

### Exterior

There are two entrances to the courtyard, with two entrances to the interior of the fort. The fort's main entrance is guarded by one [Northwatch guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Guard "Skyrim:Northwatch Guard") and is unlocked. There are two archery targets to the left of this entrance. Three more guards patrol the grounds, and three [Northwatch archers](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Archer "Skyrim:Northwatch Archer") patrol the walkways above; they all turn hostile when you trespass on the grounds. One guard is leaning by the door, another is in the camp to the left of the rear entrance, and the third is working the [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") near the camp. There is one archer standing on the battlements above the first guard, and the other two are patrolling the walkways. A back gate to the courtyard is near the fort's master-locked rear entrance, both near the forge. There is a campfire on the walkways above near a lookout platform. There are three lean-tos with unowned bedrolls near the forge, and a table opposite the locked entrance with a random one-handed weapon on top. Several barrels can be found within the courtyard, three [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes are around the forge and locked entrance, and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") is to the right of the lean-tos.

### Northwatch Keep

Prisoners have a grim future

Through the unlocked front door is a small room with two weapon plaques on the east wall holding two [steel maces](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"). Ahead is a flight of stairs that descends into a circular room with a guard and a [Northwatch mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Mage "Skyrim:Northwatch Mage") sitting at a table. There is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") among several [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") on the table, and two open crates stacked beside the table are full of more empty bottles. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on the other side of the table from the entrance, and two cupboards against the walls holding two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a single loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") on their shelves. On the far side of the room is an antechamber with a set of shelves on the left holding seven common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") and a wooden door ahead. Through the door is a passage that descends a further two flights of stairs, passing some barrels on the right, before entering another passage with a wooden table on your left, with a [woodcutters axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top and another to the right beside an unusable wooden block. The passage continues to the east, where it descends another long flight of stairs; at the bottom is an archer. Any noise made when dealing with the archers will alert a guard and a mage in the next room.

The next room is used as a bar, and contains a guard and a mage, unless they have already converged on you; one is sitting at a table, and the other is behind the bar. There are three small tables in the barroom, with a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a wedge of cheese, a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), and a bottle of wine on top of them. Against the west wall is a stack of barrels, two of which contain bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the right of these is a weapon plaque holding a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"). In the northeastern corner is a bar with five bottles of Nord mead, a bottle of wine, and an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie") on the counter, and two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), five bottles of Nord mead, two bottles of wine, and a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1")* on the shelves behind the counter. There is a passage to the north, which passes more barrels and after a couple turns opens into another passage heading west, with a cart on your right containing a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

The passage leads into a two-leveled room, with a guard to your left standing in front of a door, and two archers on the upper level, with one archer patrolling up and down. Any fighting will alert a mage who will emerge through the door on the left and who favors shock spells. This can be a challenging battle for the unaware. Through the door on the left is an L-shaped room with crates stacked up against the south wall, one of which has a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[The Legendary Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legendary_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:The Legendary Sancre Tor")* on top. Beside the crates is a table and chair with a joint of raw beef and a bottle of Nord mead on top. At the far end of the room is a large double bed with a set of shelves and a single weapon rack holding a random [one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") to the left. On the shelves is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). The mage is carrying a copy of the [Northwatch Captain's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Captain%27s_Key "Skyrim:Northwatch Captain's Key"). Returning to the previous chamber, the stairs to the upper level are against the north wall. At the top of the stairs is a cart containing a burnt corpse, and along the wall are weapon plaques holding a steel sword and mace. To the left are two tables, with a bottle of wine on top and empty bottles of wine on and around them. There is an unlocked chest to the left of a passage heading west from this level.

The passage takes a couple turns before leading to a T-junction in a wider passage with crates on either side. There is a guard sitting at a table to the right. On the table is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), and a leveled dagger. Opposite this is a row of five weapon racks holding a selection of low quality weapons. There is a lit brazier at the junction with a woodcutter's axe beside an unusable wooden block. To the left from the junction is a torture room with various torture equipment, including racks and a heated clothes iron set in coals. The room is occupied by a [Northwatch interrogator](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Interrogator "Skyrim:Northwatch Interrogator"), who carries the [Northwatch Keep key](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep_Key "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep Key") which unlocks the fort's back entrance, and who will be alerted by any fighting nearby and converge on you. In the room is an unlocked chest, a table with a bulb of garlic on top, four common books on a small shelving unit, a set of shelves holding a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), and two weapon racks on the wall that may hold a random weapon. [Thorald Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") can be found shackled to the north wall between a table covered with blood with two iron daggers and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") on top and a set of shelves holding a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and one of [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). As you approach, he will ask, "You there, what are you doing?" You will need to speak to him in order to release him.

Beside the table to the right of the junction is a wooden door that opens into a long passage with two cells on either side and two guards patrolling up and down, who may be alerted to any fighting and converge on you in the previous passage. There are two levers on the left at the start of the passage that open the cells; the cells are each master-locked and can be [lockpicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking"). Three of the cells are occupied by [unnamed prisoners](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Prisoner "Skyrim:Northwatch Prisoner"); however, they do not try to escape when released (see [Bugs](#Bugs)). At the far end is a table with a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a bottle of Nord mead, and a loaf of bread on top. Around the corner is a flight of stairs leading up, with two stacked, open crates filled with empty wine bottles and a cart containing a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic"), [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers"), and [footwraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Footwraps "Skyrim:Footwraps") on either side of the base of the stairs. At the top of the stairs is a final room containing two sets of shelves holding two bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), an iron dagger, nine common books, and three food sacks. Opposite the stairs is the master-locked door that leads outside by the forge, which can be opened using the Northwatch Keep key.

## Notes

- If the entire fort is cleared prior to the quest Missing In Action, only the inside of the fort will be reset when the quest progresses to the objectives in which you are required to save Thorald.
- With the *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* add-on installed, you can find [Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty") just northwest of here.

## Bugs

- None of the unnamed prisoners will attempt to escape from captivity, even if the dungeon is cleared and the cell doors are unlocked.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, addresses this issue. The prisoners now flee once rescued.
- [Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub") erroneously also has a Northwatch Captain's Key when she has no use for it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Northwatch Keep

# Skyrim:Northwind Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Mine.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Mine.png) | Mine: Northwind Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Mine)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Northwind_Mine "Lore:Northwind Mine")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No (see [bugs](#Bugs)) |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 12 |
| Occupants | |
| [Skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| NorthwindMineExterior01, NorthwindMineExterior02, NorthwindMine01 | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| Northwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") Southeast of [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 3 |

Northwind Mine

**Northwind Mine** is a small [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") northwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains only one zone, *[Northwind Mine](#Northwind_Mine)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

To find the mine, follow the path north out of Shor's Stone. After passing [Shor's Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Watchtower "Skyrim:Shor's Watchtower") on the right, a set of steps with a [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") ore vein will be seen on the left. Follow the path up the steps to the entrance of the mine; you may be attacked by a pair of leveled animals on the way. Alchemy ingredients, such as [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), grow east of the entrance. With *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed, a [stone quarry](/wiki/Skyrim:Stone_Quarry "Skyrim:Stone Quarry") is just west of the entrance.

### Northwind Mine

The mine has two access points, one south and one up the mountain to the north. It is inhabited by skeletons. If you are entering from the bottom, southern end of the mine, you will find a very steep incline going down into the mine. At the bottom are some skeletal remains, an abandoned handcart filled with rocks, and an iron ore vein. The mine shaft climbs upward again into the main chamber. Here two skeletons are patrolling on the wooden scaffolding. Up the ramp just inside the entrance, to the left, is an unlocked chest under the supports. To the right, just within the lantern glow, is a knapsack. The table on the west wall, at the base of the second ramp, holds a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Death Blow of Abernanit](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Blow_of_Abernanit "Skyrim:Death Blow of Abernanit")*. Between the two ramps, against the west wall is a second iron ore vein. Head up the second ramp and through a narrow passage to the top of the mine. Just before the passage widens, notice a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers a [falling boulder](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap. It is easy to disarm from this side, however, as the rocks fall into the room rather than down the passage. The last skeleton is patrolling in this area. Another iron ore vein is on the west wall, illuminated by lantern light. The passage narrows once more and turns east leading out to [Northwind Summit](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Summit "Skyrim:Northwind Summit").

## Notes

- Northwind Mine also [appears](/wiki/Online:Northwind_Mine "Online:Northwind Mine") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- None of the creatures in the mine are tagged as a boss, which prevents the location from being marked as cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Northwind Mine isn't marked as a cave, so cave-based radiant quests won't target it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- If you [fast travel](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Travel "Skyrim:Fast Travel") to the mine entrance, [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") may spawn with their feet encased in rock.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
  - They may not be able to follow you even after you zone into the mine, and you may need to move them to you via console.
  - Using [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") on the follower will knock them off the rock and allow them to follow you.
- Fast traveling to the mine while on horseback may cost you a horse. You spawn fairly high next to a rock face, and the resulting fall can kill your horse. It can also cause the player or their followers to become stuck under the rock face.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- A satchel under the scaffolding does not open and cannot be searched.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Northwind Summit

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Dragon Lair.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Dragon_Lair.png) | Dragon Lair: Northwind Summit ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwind+Summit)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Northwind_Summit "Lore:Northwind Summit")) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"), [Skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DragonLair06Exterior01, DragonLair06Exterior02, DragonLair06Exterior03, DragonLair06Exterior04 | |
| Region | |
| [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | |
| Location | |
| Northwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") South of [Northwind Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Mine "Skyrim:Northwind Mine") | |
| Special Features | |
| [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") | [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") |
| # of [Smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") | 1 |

Northwind Summit

**Northwind Summit** is a mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") northwest of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Word wall

The lair is a short distance northwest of Shor's Stone, north-northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), and far south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), on the highest point in the Rift. To access the summit, you can travel through [Northwind Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwind_Mine "Skyrim:Northwind Mine"), on the northern side of the mountain, or climb to it, starting at Shor's Stone and heading just a little ways south down the path until you see a slightly gentler mountain slope to the right. The stairs to Northwind Mine are at the northeast end of the summit. The summit is an abandoned mammoth hunter's camp with three dilapidated structures and mammoth skeletons.

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the word wall will be guarded by three [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton").

After the dragons' return, the word wall will be guarded by a leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon").

Regardless of whether [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has been completed, the word wall is against the mountain, with the boss chest just in front. A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") is to the west, between two of the structures, and an adept-locked chest is inside the farthest structure to the west, just on the precipice of the summit.

## Notes

- A [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") is above the Northwind Mine entrance.

## Bugs

- If the dragon crash lands during your battle, the scripted terrain alterations may make it impossible to enter or leave the northwestern cabin (the one containing the locked chest), meaning that if you are inside, you will be unable to get out.
  - If you can find a way to kill the dragon while trapped in the cabin (for example, by using a follower or summoned creature), you will be able to exit via fast travel after leaving combat.

# Skyrim:NPCs

## Overview

**NPC** (**Non-Player Character**) is a generic term for all humanoids (of various [races](/wiki/Skyrim:Races "Skyrim:Races")), other than you, that are encountered while playing [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

The difference between NPCs and other [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") is somewhat blurry in Skyrim. One key difference is in [trapping their souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)"): NPC souls cannot be trapped into ordinary [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"); only [Black Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") or [Azura's Star (Black)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star_(item) "Skyrim:The Black Star (item)") can be used.

[Classes](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") are still used by NPCs, despite being inaccessible to you.

## Named NPCs

There are many **named NPCs** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). These people are all listed on the [People](/wiki/Skyrim:People "Skyrim:People") page. All quest-givers, [trainers](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers"), and [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants") in the game, as well most of the people in cities and towns are named characters.

Some named characters are deemed to be Essential ("unkillable"). If these characters are attacked, they will fall to their knees and surrender when they near zero [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health"). After a few moments, they will rise up with full health, and will reengage their enemies until the latter parties are dead or out of the area. Protected characters, on the other hand, can be attacked and killed by you but not by NPCs (however, a bug means that poisons can kill even Protected characters). Most NPCs can be killed, but there may be consequences later.

Special categories include:

- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers")
- [Essential NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs")
- [Protected NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:Protected_NPCs "Skyrim:Protected NPCs")

## Generic NPCs

There are also many **generic NPCs** in the game, most of which are randomly generated. If one dies for whatever reason, the game will eventually generate a new random replacement.

Friendly NPCs include:

- [Alik'r Warriors](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Warrior "Skyrim:Alik'r Warrior")

- [Treasure Hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Hunter_(dead) "Skyrim:Treasure Hunter (dead)")

Various other humanoid enemies (e.g., [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [dragon priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest"), [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven")) are not NPCs, meaning they do not have black [souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls").

## Console IDs

All characters in the game have two distinct [FormIDs](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") that can be used in conjunction with [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands: a **BaseID** and a **RefID**. Most console commands will accept only one of the two types of IDs: the BaseID is generally used in cases where you want to spawn a new copy of an object, whereas the RefID is generally used in cases where you want to interact with an existing copy of an object. The BaseID points or refers to the immutable prototype or template of an object; the RefID points or refers to the actual in-game working copy of the object.

Although this RefID/BaseID distinction exists for all objects in the game, it is particularly important for all of the game's unique NPCs. Most of the game scripts use RefIDs (via the associated EditorID) to control unique NPCs. This means that if you use the `placeatme <BaseID>` command to spawn a new copy (with a new RefID) of, for example, [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern"), the new copy of Esbern will be ignored by most of the quest scripts. Your clone may have the correct dialogues and appearance, but many quest updates triggered by Esbern will not be triggered by your clone.

Therefore, when using the console with unique NPCs you should always **avoid** the `placeatme` command. All of this site's NPC pages provide the NPC's RefID, as long as the ID is not randomly generated, which should be used to locate or modify the existing copy of the NPC. For example, to move a missing NPC to your location, use:

- `prid <RefId>`
- `moveto player`

If the NPC is not visible after those commands, then the character may have been disabled, so type:

- `enable`

Or if the character is dead:

- `resurrect 1`

If you would prefer to move your character to the location of an NPC (instead of vice versa), you can instead use the command:

- `player.moveto <RefId>`

## NPC Statistics

The behavior of an NPC is controlled by a variety of NPC-specific statistics. [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") is listed on a separate page.

### Aggression

There are four possible values for aggression. Together with the [faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") relationship combat modifier this governs whether the NPC initiates combat.

- **0**: Unaggressive. Attacks nobody unless provoked.
- **1**: Aggressive. Attacks enemies on sight.
- **2**: Very Aggressive. Attacks enemies and neutral on sight.
- **3**: Frenzied. Attacks anybody on sight.

### Assistance

Assistance determines whether an NPC will help in combat.

- **0**: Will not help anyone.
- **1**: Will only help Allies.
- **2**: Will help Friends and Allies.

### Confidence

There are five possible values for confidence:

- **0**: Cowardly. Always flees from battle at low health.
- **1**: Cautious. Attacks only lower level enemies.
- **2**: Average. Avoids higher level creatures.
- **3**: Brave. Attacks unless being outmatched by the opponent.
- **4**: Foolhardy. Attacks any type of enemy and fights to the death.

### Morality

Morality determines whether or not an NPC will commit various [crimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime"), and controls whether or not a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") will agree to do certain requested actions. There are four possible values for morality:

- **0**: Any Crime. NPC is willing to commit any requested crime.
- **1**: Violence Against Enemies. NPC is willing to commit violence against enemies, as well as property crimes. NPC is not willing to attack innocent people.
- **2**: Property Crime Only. The only crimes the NPC will commit are property crimes (i.e., theft).
- **3**: No Crime. NPC is not willing to commit any crimes. Followers with this morality will still not report crimes that they witness you committing (with the exception of crimes against them, such as stealing items owned by the follower).

## Notes

- If you complete one or more of an NPC's quests, they will often greet you by saying *"You've been a good friend to me. That means something."* or another similar phrase indicating their [affection](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"). This conveys certain benefits, such as allowing you to take some low value items from their dwelling, or making some NPCs available to become a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") or [spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage"). An NPC's disposition may also give rise to certain [world interactions](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") when they see you.

# Skyrim:Odfel's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

Odfel's House

**Odfel's House** is a house in the small mining settlement of  [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone").

It is the home of two local miners, [Odfel](/wiki/Skyrim:Odfel "Skyrim:Odfel") and [Grogmar gro-Burzag](/wiki/Skyrim:Grogmar_gro-Burzag "Skyrim:Grogmar gro-Burzag"). It consists of one area only, *[Odfel's House](#Odfel.27s_House)*.

Odfel and Grogmar each occupy a different half of the building, and spend all of their time arguing about who cleans up the most, at times even betting about it. Despite the name of the house, it seems Odfel desires to leave it to Grogmar and build a new one.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Grogmar gro-Burzag](/wiki/Skyrim:Grogmar_gro-Burzag "Skyrim:Grogmar gro-Burzag")  [Odfel](/wiki/Skyrim:Odfel "Skyrim:Odfel") |

## Odfel's House

Odfel's House interior

The front door opens to the sight of a sizzling fire and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") that marks the center of the house. In front of the pot is a small dinner table with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a slice of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a copy of *[Rising Threat, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. IV")*. Underneath the table lie a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). Next to the fireplace is a set of shelves with beverages, four bottles of alto wine, and four bottles of regular [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine").

The southern part of the house clearly belongs to Odfel, although both owned beds stand there. At the foot of the bed in the southeastern corner sits a chest with few valuables. Between the beds is an end table with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top and an empty wardrobe. Between the beds and the front door is a dresser with some [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with several alchemical [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") on top: four clusters of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three pine thrush eggs, two samples of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and two samples of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Above the dresser hang three garlic braids, and one portion each of dried elves ear and dried frost mirriam.

The northern part of the house holds little of interest and is more messy than its southern counterpart, with the exception of three food barrels and a bottle of Nord mead and one bottle of alto wine on the table. Also, hidden in a bucket on the table, are three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). Above the table hang one dried frost mirriam, one dried elves ear, and two garlic braids. From a hook hangs some game as well, three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

Ogmund's House

**Ogmund's House** is a small home in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

It is the home of local bard and [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") trainer [Ogmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund "Skyrim:Ogmund"), who usually hangs out at the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn"). It is located next door to [Endon's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon%27s_House "Skyrim:Endon's House") and directly above [Arnleif and Sons Trading Company](/wiki/Skyrim:Arnleif_and_Sons_Trading_Company "Skyrim:Arnleif and Sons Trading Company").

It consists of one area, *[Ogmund's House](#Ogmund.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Ogmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund "Skyrim:Ogmund") [Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Speech (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Speech (Expert)") |

## Related Quests

- **[Search and Seizure](/wiki/Skyrim:Search_and_Seizure "Skyrim:Search and Seizure")**: Find evidence of a [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") [worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund "Skyrim:Ogmund") for the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

## Ogmund's House

The interior of the house

Upon entering you will see this is one open room with a dining/kitchen area to the west, a raised storage in front and another raised area for sleeping to the east.

Immediately on your left as you enter is a stone shelf containing a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") sample, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a cup and a plate. To the right is a barrel with four [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") samples on the floor around it. Further along the wall next to the dining table is a copy of the book *[Fall from Glory](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_from_Glory "Skyrim:Fall from Glory")*, a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") sample and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). On the dining table is a lute, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and one of [Alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a goblet, two bowls, two cups and various foodstuffs. Behind the dining table to the west is the kitchen area with more foodstuffs on stone shelves with a portion of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and a garlic braid hanging from these. There is also a rack with two rabbits and a pheasant. There is a cook pot behind the table.

As you climb the stairs to the storage area there is a stool with a lit candle and goblet, a chair and flute next to this and a barrel behind. Against the north wall is a stone sideboard containing a mead barrel, a plate, more food, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a drum, [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") and a chest (this will contain the object of the quest, if that has been started). An [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") are on the floor to the right of the chest, next to a practice dummy.

The sleeping area contains a bed with a chest, a sack and a copy of *[Azura and the Box](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura_and_the_Box "Skyrim:Azura and the Box")* to the left. To the right of the bed is an end table with a flute on top, while a small stone table further to the right holds a copy of *[The Song of Pelinal, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v3 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v3")*, one medium and one large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a goblet, a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") and two bottles of wine. To the left of the exit is a stone shelf containing a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") on a plate, with a basket containing more foodstuffs on the floor beside it.

## Notes

- There is a "Loot" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the top left of the entrance door.

Olava the Feeble's House Exterior

**Olava the Feeble's House** is a small house in the southern part of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It is located right behind [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome").

It is the residence of elderly seer [Olava the Feeble](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava_the_Feeble "Skyrim:Olava the Feeble") and consists of one area only, *[Olava the Feeble's House](#Olava_the_Feeble.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Olava the Feeble](/wiki/Skyrim:Olava_the_Feeble "Skyrim:Olava the Feeble") |

## Olava the Feeble's House

Olava's House

The house is among the smallest houses in Whiterun and contains very little of value. The front door opens to a huge open fire with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and some hanging [Dried Elves Ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"). The table on the left holds a [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") while the single shelf on the wall holds two [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment") and the end table contains a few pieces of gold.

To the right of the front door is Olava's owned bed and a cupboard with clutter. On the shelves above sits some food and, a coin purse, a book *[The Holds of Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:The_Holds_of_Skyrim "Lore:The Holds of Skyrim")*, and a sack with food or [Salt](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). The small alcove to the west has a chest with some gold and pelts, an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). On the adjacent shelves, above the two food barrels, sits a sample of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), a [potion of brief invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine").

## Notes

- There is an  "Empty") Empty [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") on the left of the door, due to the lack of valuable items inside.

Old Attius Farm Cellar

**Old Attius Farm Cellar** is a cellar located underneath the ruined house at [Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm"). It can be accessed via a trapdoor hidden within the ruined wooden farmhouse.

You will follow a suspicious [Redoran Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") to this location during the related quest. He will enter the cellar to meet with the [Buyer](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer "Skyrim:Buyer"), a mysterious individual seeking to purchase the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").

## Related Quests

- **[Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Ambush a meeting to retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").

## Old Attius Farm Cellar

Cellar interior

The cellar is smoke-filled and contains nothing but broken furniture and a few burning candles.

# Skyrim:Old Attius Farm

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Farm.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Farm.png) | Farm: Old Attius Farm ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Old+Attius+Farm)) | | |

| South-southeast of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") North of [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") | |

Old Attius Farm

**Old Attius Farm** is an abandoned Imperial [farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Farms "Skyrim:Farms") south-southeast of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

The first time you approach the farm, [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") will be battling three [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"). Once the ash spawn are dead, you will receive a miscellaneous quest objective to talk to the captain. Speaking with him initiates the quest [March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead"). Outside the house is a dead [Redoran guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard_(dead) "Skyrim:Redoran Guard (dead)") that carries an [Elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword"), [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Bow "Skyrim:Elven Bow"), and arrows, and a full set of [Bonemold armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold#Bonemold_Armor "Skyrim:Bonemold") (the chest armor is the [pauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold#Bonemold_Pauldron_Armor "Skyrim:Bonemold") version).

The [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") adds a trapdoor to the house leading to **[Old Attius Farm Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm_Cellar "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm Cellar")**. You will need to enter the cellar during the quest [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware").

## Related Quests

- **[Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Ambush a meeting to retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").
- **[March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead")**: Stop the [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") attacks on [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

## Walkthrough

The farm is along the road leading south from Raven Rock. There is little left of the farmhouse, but the plants in the two gardens still grow among the weeds. There is an empty chest on the porch, and a [trama root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root") grows through the back wall. In the left-hand garden are ten [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam") (including one growing outside the fence), three [scathecraws](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw"), and a trama root. In the right-hand garden are eight ash yams, two scathecraws, and a trama root. An additional seven trama roots grow in the immediate vicinity, with a large number of scathecraw plants between the farm and Raven Rock.

| Crops | Plants |
| --- | --- |
| 18 [Ash Yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam") | 5 [Scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw")  10 [Trama Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root") |

## Notes

- Directly west of the farm is an [unmarked location on a small island](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Solstheim#Reavers.27_Folly "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Solstheim"). Three [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") plants and a [heart stone deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit") are found on the island. In the middle is a small camp with two bloodied bedrolls, a [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a box holding two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and a pair of [bonemold gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Bonemold Gauntlets"), a food barrel, and two dead [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"). There is a boat on the southern side of the island, with a sack inside and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on a crate nearby. Beware, as three [ash hoppers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Hopper "Skyrim:Ash Hopper") will emerge from the ground as you explore the camp.
- According to Captain Veleth, the farm was destroyed by the eruption of [Red Mountain](/wiki/Lore:Red_Mountain "Lore:Red Mountain") almost two hundred years ago, in [4E 5](/wiki/Lore:Fourth_Era#4E_5 "Lore:Fourth Era").
- The dead Redoran Guard's inventory replenishes itself when the farm resets.

# Skyrim:Old Friends

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Krusty](/wiki/User:Krusty "User:Krusty"), checked by [Velyanthe](/wiki/User:Velyanthe "User:Velyanthe") |
