[Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") attack [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)").
2. Investigate the graveyard near Tel Mithryn using the [Ring of Tracking](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth%27s_Ring_of_Tracking "Skyrim:Neloth's Ring of Tracking").
3. Return to Neloth.
4. Go to [Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower") and kill [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril").
5. Return to Neloth for your reward.

### The Ring of Tracking

Something is wrong at the graveyard.

With his steward [killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"), his tower [withered](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House"), and several other annoyances related to [Ash Spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"), master Telvanni wizard [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") finally loses his patience when three Ash Spawn attack his [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"). Once you have killed the Ash Spawn, enter the tower and talk to the wizard who will reveal it is finally time to investigate who is behind the attacks: *"Yes. I have enemies. Legions of them back in Morrowind. However, in this case I have reason to believe it is someone in Solstheim."* When asked if he wants the responsible persons dead, he will respond: *"Not yet. That may come later. First I need to identify the culprit. I've enchanted this ring to find the source of the attacks. Here, take it."* He will then hand you the [Ring of Tracking](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth%27s_Ring_of_Tracking "Skyrim:Neloth's Ring of Tracking") and explain that you need to wear it in order for it to work. The ring was enchanted with a bit of ash from the last Ash Spawn attack and will allow you to follow the magical link back to the source of the summoned Ash Spawn. However, it has its disadvantages: *"The link is weak, so you'll have to be within about a hundred feet of the source."* Neloth will then order you to walk around the grounds while wearing the ring. Equip the ring and leave the tower behind.

### From Beyond the Grave

Once outside, head north to the field of mushrooms and then east towards a lone evergreen tree at the shore, until you reach [a small graveyard](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&x=81000&y=28000) inhabited by a peaceful [netch](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch "Skyrim:Netch") family. With the ring equipped, one of the coffins will have a clear bluish glow. As you approach the graveyard, the expected Ash Spawn will appear and attack, so fight it and investigate Ildari's sarcophagus. The coffin lacks a dead body, and contains a [staff of calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Calm "Skyrim:Staff of Calm") and a [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone"). Grab the stone and return to Neloth in the tower.

*"She lives. Seek her in Highpoint Tower."*

If you have already played through [March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead"), the name Ildari should be familiar, due to the [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal") you [found](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead#Falx_Carius "Skyrim:March of the Dead") when you helped [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth") with his Ash Spawn problems in [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth"). When you hand the stone to Neloth, he will be quite surprised and reveal [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril") to be a former apprentice of his: *"Ildari? Then it's my own fault. She was my apprentice before Talvas. She volunteered for one of my experiments involving heart stones. It was quite annoying when she died."* He will then elaborate on how she died: *"My necropsies of Spriggans led me to believe that a heart stone could be implanted in a person's chest, granting them great power. I was considering replacing my heart with a heart stone. Fortunately Ildari offered to let me operate on her first. Of course this was before your [briarheart expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:Briarheart_Necropsy "Skyrim:Briarheart Necropsy"). Now I know that I did the surgery all wrong."* When you tell him that the sarcophagus was empty, he will be quick to put two and two together: *"That's impossible. Wait... unless she didn't actually die! The heart stone could have kept her right at the edge of life and death. Could it be? Could Ildari still be alive? Could she be my nemesis? Wait a moment while I cast a more specific divination."* Moments afterward, Neloth will cast a spell that will light up most of the tower, and will start to talk in a completely different voice, as if a spirit is talking through him: *"She lives. Seek her in Highpoint Tower."* Neloth will then return to normal and immediately order you to head to said tower, as he can't be bothered himself. The last thing he will say is: *"Go rip that thrice cursed heart stone from her chest."*

### Highpoint Tower

[Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower")

[Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower") is located north of Ildari's former hideout, [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth"), southeast from [Brodir Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Brodir_Grove "Skyrim:Brodir Grove"). Enter the tower via a tunnel on the north side; fight the guarding Ash Spawn and head up the stairs. Once inside, head down the spiral staircase. Two stories down, you will come across a table with *[Ildari's Journal, vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal,_vol._I "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal, vol. I")*, where a weakened Ildari Sarothril describes how she was saved by some miners, and how she is planning her revenge on her former master back in Tel Mithryn. Continue down the stairs and head west until you reach a chamber, filled with egg sacks from various spiders. As you enter the chamber, beware of the [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") to the north, as it can complicate your battle against the spiders considerably. Multiple paths are available here; the tunnel to the south leads to a huge spiders nest and some useful veins, while the tunnel with the spellcaster trap is the way towards your goal. At the first intersection, enter the room with the three Ash Spawn and pick the fight, then proceed to the north and remove the [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") from yet another spellcaster trap. In the next chamber, a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") triggers some [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders"). Use the [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") if needed, and beware the [elemental rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Rune "Skyrim:Elemental Rune") in the center of the room. Head down the eastern path until you reach the rare sight of an elemental rune on the wall, with tunnels leading north and south. Head south until you reach a jail-like area with several cells.

The table in the center of the jail has *[Ildari's Journal, vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal,_vol._II "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal, vol. II")*, detailing how Ildari was able to survive Neloth's operation, and how her paranoia against the very people who saved her slowly increases due to the [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") implemented in her chest. She also describes how she will keep a few of them as prisoners for future experiments. Before long, [Niyya](/wiki/Skyrim:Niyya "Skyrim:Niyya") will call to you from her cell. When you pick the lock, she will come out and thank you: *"Thank you for rescuing me. That witch was going to kill me soon, I just know it."* She will then tell you the background: *"We were digging in these mines when she found us. She was hurt so bad. We took pity on her and nursed her back to health. She repaid our kindness by attacking us in the middle of the night. Those of us that didn't die were made prisoners."* She will go on to explain how Ildari used her saviors for experiments and will angrily encourage you to make her suffer a painful death. She will then rush towards the exit, with plans to leave Solstheim for good.

### Kill the Witch

An [Ash Guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian") is born

Return to the elemental rune, head north and locate the passage to the east. A wooden ramp leads down while a wooden catwalk goes forward with a crate holding meat on top. Follow the catwalk to find two orichalcum veins to mine. Return to the ramp to proceed to the next chamber. In the next chamber is a glowing [sapphire geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Geode "Skyrim:Sapphire Geode") on the ground, while another can be reached by traversing up the wooden structure. There is another orichalcum ore veins on the other side of the room from the first geode and a gold ore vein near the wooden structure's ramp. Proceed forward in a northwestern direction until you reach a large chamber with a strange device in the middle. Before long, Ildari will speak from her spot above: *"You've gone far enough. Neloth is a fool to think he could send some low life to finish me off."* With these words, she will activate the device, creating an [Ash Guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian"). At this point, numerous Ash Spawn will emerge as well, so pick the tough battle and dispose of the Ash Guardian. With the area cleared, start traversing the woodworks to the southwest and explore the path thoroughly for some treasure and ingredients. Once you reach a ledge with a table and a random rare book, loot the shelves for various potions and other loot and read through  *[Ildari's Journal, vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal,_vol._III "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal, vol. III")*. In this final volume, Ildari describes how she patiently started getting her vengeance on Neloth, and how she is responsible for the death of [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas"), and the withering of Tel Mithryn tower. Proceed to climb the woodworks and follow the tunnel leading southwest, killing all the Ash Spawn that emerge on the way.

[Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril")

Once you reach a broken-down wall, two paths are available. The path to the northeast leads to a dead end and an open chest with some minor loot while the adjacent path leads to a wooden bridge. Cross the bridge and follow the tunnel as it twists and turns until you reach the final chamber, the lair of [Ildari Sarothril](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari_Sarothril "Skyrim:Ildari Sarothril"). Ildari will be on the woodworks above and will have two [elemental traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Elemental_Traps "Skyrim:Traps") shooting at you at all times. Dodge the magical attacks and locate the entrance to the southwest and follow the path as it leads you to the second floor. Ildari will now start attacking you. She is a powerful sorceress with several spells at her disposal, although she will mainly use her [staff of lightning bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts") to attack you. After the battle, Ildari will kneel down. With Ildari helpless, follow Neloth's orders and rip out the heart stone from her chest, forever ending her vengeful scheme. Once everything is quiet, claim a reward from the boss-leveled chest and search the shelves for jewelry, ingredients, and other loot. Activate the lever and watch the spikes disappear from the entrance to the southeast. Head up the stairs, to the very top of the tower, and pull the chain for a very quick escape route back to Solstheim.

### Reward

Back in Tel Mithryn, Neloth will be happy to see the end of his nemesis and will, for once, reward you accordingly: *"Well, well. You have proven to be a more valuable ally than I anticipated. I have a staff for you, but I would also like to make you a member of my household. A member of House Telvanni. No need to thank me. I know you are overwhelmed with gratitude."* He will then hand you a random, leveled staff and tell you that your new membership of the household means very little for the time being, although he will promise you a bed and a chest in his tower (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Notes

- Highpoint Tower is blocked by ash until this quest has been initiated.
- A complete set of [Skaal equipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Boots "Skyrim:Skaal Boots") can be obtained in Highpoint Tower during this quest, atop the earthen archway in the tunnel past the alchemy lab area.
- If your Archery skill is good enough, you can kill Ildari while she is talking before the Ash Guardian is raised as she stands in the open on a platform beyond the summoning circle.
- Ildari can be pickpocketed if you're in stealth mode when you rip her heart out. The heart will be removed once you close the menu.

## Bugs

- Even though Neloth tells you he will keep a bed and chest for you, there is not a chest specifically for you and all of the beds are still owned.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.3, fixes this bug.
  - The bed in the Steward's House is unowned from the start, although [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas") (or later [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi")) usually sleeps in it.
- Neloth may fail to cast the more specific spell to find Ildari, so the quest marker remains as "Talk to Neloth".
  - Leaving and reentering Tel Mithryn may allow Neloth to cast the spell, so the quest can progress. Attacking Neloth may also work, although this will result in a bounty.
  - If Neloth is in the enchanting room, push/bump/shove him into the main room.
- The animation for ripping out Ildari's heart may not activate.
  - Wait at least 10 seconds after you're given the prompt to rip Ildari's heart out
- The game may crash when attempting to rip out Ildari's heart.
  - Save your game near Ildari as a precautionary measure.
- If you have opened Ildari's sarcophagus prior to this quest, the heart stone may not be inside it when the quest begins, preventing you from completing it.
  - If you open the sarcophagus prior to the quest you will find a staff. The heart stone will be present once you have started the quest.
- The Ring of Tracking may lead you to an invisible object near Tel Mithryn instead of Ildari's sarcophagus.
  - Activating the sarcophagus will continue the quest normally.
- Upon putting Ildari in Bleedout, the player is given a perk that enables the prompt to "Rip Heart Out", and that adds a multiplier of 0.01 to the magnitude of Illusion effects on the player. This persists until the perk is removed upon killing Ildari. This notably makes the [Ring of Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Khajiit "Skyrim:Ring of Khajiit") and [Ring of the Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_the_Wind "Skyrim:Ring of the Wind") very weak. **?**
  - The perk can be removed via `player.removeperk 0403d597`, it will be reacquired when Ildari is next put into Bleedout.

## Quest Stages

| Old Friends (DLC2TT2) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | Neloth is being attacked by an unknown assailant. He gave me a ring that will identify the source of the attacks. If I walk around the grounds of Tel Mithryn, I might find a clue. *Objective 100:* Find the source of the attacks |
| 200 |  | Neloth is being attacked by an unknown assailant. He gave me a ring that identified the source of the attacks as a heart stone hidden in the grave of Ildari Sarothril. *Objective 200:* Talk to Neloth |
| 300 |  | Neloth is being attacked by an unknown assailant. I discovered the source of the attacks was a heart stone hidden in Ildari Sarothril's grave. Neloth has divined that his former apprentice is still alive and seeking vengeance on him. Neloth asked me to track down and kill Ildari. *Objective 400:* Kill Ildari |
| 500 |  | Neloth's former apprentice, Ildari Sarothril, was covertly attacking him. Deep under Highpoint Tower I confronted Ildari and killed her. *Objective 500:* Talk to Neloth |
| 600 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 5, 10, 250, 310, 400.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TT2 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TT2`.

Old Hroldan Inn

**Old Hroldan Inn** is a remote inn in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") where [Tiber Septim](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim") once stayed. It is operated by [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis") with the help of her young son [Skuli](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuli "Skyrim:Skuli"). Eydis claims her husband is fighting in the war, though there appears to be some doubt as to which side he fights for. [Leontius Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius") spends all day working outside on various menial tasks, and offers no services.

The inn is north of the road from [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") to [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") near where the road crosses the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").

Being in an isolated location in an otherwise desolate settlement, the inn touts its ties to Tiber Septim's conquest of Hroldan, and claims to have the same bed the young general slept in the night before the battle which they offer to their patrons.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper")[Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") \*  [Leontius Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius") †  [Skuli](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuli "Skyrim:Skuli") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink") |

\* Only while [The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan") is active.
† Becomes innkeeper only if Eydis is dead.

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

#### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Rogatus's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Rogatus's Letter")**: Deliver a letter to a [farmer's](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogatus_Salvius "Skyrim:Rogatus Salvius") [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius").

### Exterior

The path to the inn is on your right when traveling from [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") to [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") a few paces before you cross the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"). Along the path that passes the inn are a couple tree stumps with [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus growing on them as well as several of the [juniper trees](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") that abound in the region. The path continues past the inn and eventually joins another path that goes from [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole") to near [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") before petering out. There is a patch of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus growing to the left of the front porch, and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") are south of the entrance. On the porch to the left of the entrance are three [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, and the [Fishing Map - The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Map_-_The_Reach "Skyrim:Fishing Map - The Reach") is on the right barrel.

### Old Hroldan Inn

The entrance leads directly into the common room, which like most inns in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), has a long firepit down the middle of the room, five long wooden tables against the side walls, and a counter at the far end. There are several barrels containing foodstuffs around the room and three doorways off the main room, two to the northwest and one to the southeast. The tables are laden with a selection of bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a couple loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and either [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") or [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), except for the table in the western corner, which has a couple [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and several pieces of cheese instead of the eggs. There is a basket beside the firepit containing three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"). The counter, which is at the northeast end of the room and is where [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis") spends her days, has a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, several pieces of cheese, and a copy of *[Final Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:Final_Lesson "Skyrim:Final Lesson")* on top, and two more bottles of wine, a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), and five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") underneath. Behind the counter, along the northeast wall, are a couple large vats and a set of shelves holding three bottles of alto wine and five bottles of wine, with a pile of firewood to the right. There are several racks hanging from the ceiling in front of the vats and shelves holding a total of eleven [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). On either side of the doorway to the southeast are two sets of shelves holding a total of two bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), four loaves of bread, and three bunches of elves ear.

The large bedroom to the southeast is Tiber Septim's room, and is where Eydis claims [Tiber Septim](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim") slept on his first night after seizing Old Hroldan from the [Witchmen of High Rock](/wiki/Lore:Reachmen "Lore:Reachmen"). The battle is famous for being where Hjalti Early-Beard (later Tiber Septim) earned the name Talos Stormcrown, when he used the [Thu'um](/wiki/Skyrim:Thu%27um "Skyrim:Thu'um") to break the settlement's defenses. Eydis will rent you the room for 10 septims a day. The room is the one to the southeast, and contains a large double bed by the southeast wall with an end table on either side, one of which has a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:Battle of Sancre Tor")* on top, while the other has a bottle of wine on top. There are also an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed, a long unlocked chest against the southwest wall, and a kettle in the southern corner containing a copy of *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")*. In the western corner, along the northwest wall, is an owned single bed. The first time you sleep in this room will initiate the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan") to help an ancient ghost.

Opposite the Tiber Septim room are two more smaller bedrooms. The bedroom to the left contains an owned single bed in the southwestern corner with a round wooden table and chair beside it and a novice-locked chest at the foot of the bed, with a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") against the northwest wall. On the table are a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a copy of *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*. The bedroom to the right contains an owned single bed in the northeastern corner with a round wooden table and chair beside it, a novice-locked chest at the foot of the bed, and a dresser against the northeast wall. There is a copy of *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")* on the table.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn food |
| 1 | [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") |

## Notes

- Unused game data indicates the inn was originally intended to be part of a larger settlement known as **Old Hroldan**.
  - Several internal references indicate the inn was originally named the "Hanged Man's Inn", rather than the Old Hroldan Inn.
  - An [unfinished quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfinished_Quests "Skyrim:Unfinished Quests") tied to the location reveals that at one point, a mine (the name of which is unknown) and at least four other NPCs were to be present: two Reachman miners and cousins named **Lioch** and **Maeduin**, a Nord mine overseer named **Heggvild**, and an unnamed fourth NPC who was possibly one of the settlement's higher-ups.
- If you take the path to the north into the mountains, it'll lead towards the village of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). Along the way you'll encounter a small camp with the lovers Karan and [Talvur](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvur "Skyrim:Talvur"). Unfortunately, they've been killed (possibly by the [predator](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") nearby), but *[Karan's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Karan%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Karan's Journal")* indicates they have a stash hidden right nearby in a stump. Later, a [Shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara") can be found here.

Old Hroldan Inn

**Old Hroldan Inn** is a remote inn in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") where [Tiber Septim](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim") once stayed. It is operated by [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis") with the help of her young son [Skuli](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuli "Skyrim:Skuli"). Eydis claims her husband is fighting in the war, though there appears to be some doubt as to which side he fights for. [Leontius Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius") spends all day working outside on various menial tasks, and offers no services.

The inn is north of the road from [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") to [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") near where the road crosses the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River").

Being in an isolated location in an otherwise desolate settlement, the inn touts its ties to Tiber Septim's conquest of Hroldan, and claims to have the same bed the young general slept in the night before the battle which they offer to their patrons.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper")[Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") \*  [Leontius Salvius](/wiki/Skyrim:Leontius_Salvius "Skyrim:Leontius Salvius") †  [Skuli](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuli "Skyrim:Skuli") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink") |

\* Only while [The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan") is active.
† Becomes innkeeper only if Eydis is dead.

### Old Hroldan Inn

There is a copy of *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")* on the table.

# Skyrim:Once A Hunter

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Track down a hunter with a dangerous past.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Started by reading [Guard Dossier: Aesrael](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dossier:_Aesrael "Skyrim:Guard Dossier: Aesrael") or [Guard's Bounty Letter Draft](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Bounty_Letter_Draft "Skyrim:Guard's Bounty Letter Draft") |
| Location(s): | [Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks"), [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge") |
| Reward: | Set of [Elven Hunter Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Hunter_Armor "Skyrim:Elven Hunter Armor") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE064\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Elven Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Elven_Hunter "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Elven Hunter") |

A dangerous bandit has come to Skyrim.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read [Guard Dossier: Aesrael](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dossier:_Aesrael "Skyrim:Guard Dossier: Aesrael") or [Guard's Bounty Letter Draft](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Bounty_Letter_Draft "Skyrim:Guard's Bounty Letter Draft") at the [Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks").
2. Go to [Aesrael](/wiki/Skyrim:Aesrael "Skyrim:Aesrael")'s camp near [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge") and obtain his key.
3. Open Aesrael's chest and pick up the Elven Hunter Armor.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Rifle through papers in the guard barracks.

Aesrael's camp

To begin this quest travel to the [Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks"). Once there, read *[Guard Dossier: Aesrael](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dossier:_Aesrael "Skyrim:Guard Dossier: Aesrael")* or *[Guard's Bounty Letter Draft](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Bounty_Letter_Draft "Skyrim:Guard's Bounty Letter Draft")* which will grant you the quest and direct you to the forests west of [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge").

Once there, locate [Aesrael](/wiki/Skyrim:Aesrael "Skyrim:Aesrael")'s camp. You must obtain [Aesrael's Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Aesrael%27s_Key "Skyrim:Aesrael's Key") from him, either by pickpocketing or killing him. Note that both Aesrael and his pet wolf [Dusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Dusk "Skyrim:Dusk") will be hostile.

After the key is obtained, use it to open the chest near his tent, which will contain the [Elven Hunter Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Hunter_Armor "Skyrim:Elven Hunter Armor"), [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Hunter_Boots "Skyrim:Elven Hunter Boots"), and [Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Hunter_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Elven Hunter Gauntlets"), as well a copy of *[The Crimson Dirks, v7](/wiki/Lore:The_Crimson_Dirks,_v7 "Lore:The Crimson Dirks, v7")* and some leveled loot.

## Notes

- The Fishing side quest [Clear-Headed](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear-Headed "Skyrim:Clear-Headed") overlaps here in the barracks.
- The location of Aesrael's camp overlaps with the final location of the [Redguard Elite Armaments](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Elite_Armaments "Skyrim:Redguard Elite Armaments") creation that is at the entrance to Sunderstone Gorge. So his wolf "Dusk" may attack while doing that quest.
- This is the lightest armor in the game.
- After the quest is completed, pieces of Elven Hunter Armor can appear in leveled lists of loot (such as the leveled cuirass in the last chamber of [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow#Shroud_Hearth_Depths "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow")). It will also be added to the inventory of [Blacksmiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith"), who will begin selling pieces of Elven Hunter Armor. In contrast to most other alternative armors, it will not appear in the crafting menu, merchant chests, or the inventory of NPCs before this.

## Quest Stages

| Once A Hunter (ccBGSSSE064\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | At the barracks of Falkreath, I found information implicating a hunter to the south *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* of Sunderstone Gorge. Apparently in another life, he was a notorious bandit. I should investigate the camps in the area and see what I can find. *Objective :* Kill Aesrael |
| 10 |  | At the barracks of Falkreath, I found information implicating a hunter to the south *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* of Sunderstone Gorge. Apparently in another life, he was a notorious bandit. After reading the note, I found a camp in the area and killed the High Elf. *Objective :* Search Aesrael's body |
| 30 |  | *Objective :* Search Aesrael's chest |
| 100 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE064_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE064_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Onmund's Request

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | Onmund's friendship and availability as follower/spouse |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund")) |
| ID: | MGRAppOnmund01 |
| Required Items: | [Grand Staff of Charming](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Staff_of_Charming "Skyrim:Grand Staff of Charming") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") | | |

Onmund's Amulet

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund").
2. Speak with [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir").
3. Retrieve the [Grand Staff of Charming](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Staff_of_Charming "Skyrim:Grand Staff of Charming") from a random location.
4. Return the staff to Enthir.
5. Return the amulet to Onmund.

## Detailed Walkthrough

By now, you will have gotten to know [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund"), the friendly and singular [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). He has traded his family amulet to [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") but now regrets his decision. Onmund will not tell you what he traded the amulet for, but asks for your help in getting his property back.

Speak with Enthir about this. Enthir offers you a deal: he will trade the amulet if you retrieve the [Grand Staff of Charming](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Staff_of_Charming "Skyrim:Grand Staff of Charming") from a certain location. The randomly selected location will usually include a boss-level caster foe guarding a chest containing the staff.

To complete the quest, retrieve the staff and return it to Enthir, who will in turn give you Onmund's amulet. Return the amulet to Onmund who will be grateful. The only reward for completing the quest is Onmund's friendship; once you return his amulet, he becomes available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), as well as a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

Possible staff locations are:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund") [Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope") [Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond") [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") | [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne") [Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass") [Falkreath Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Watchtower "Skyrim:Falkreath Watchtower") [Haemar's Shame](/wiki/Skyrim:Haemar%27s_Shame "Skyrim:Haemar's Shame") [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep") [Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion") [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum") [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge") | [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep") [Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave") [Potema's Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Potema%27s_Catacombs "Skyrim:Potema's Catacombs") [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave") | [Movarth's Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Movarth%27s_Lair "Skyrim:Movarth's Lair") | [Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl") | [Boulderfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Boulderfall_Cave "Skyrim:Boulderfall Cave") [Redwater Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Redwater_Den "Skyrim:Redwater Den")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave") [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") [Moldering Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moldering_Ruins "Skyrim:Moldering Ruins")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave") [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild") |

## Notes

- With a sufficiently high [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill or the [Amulet of Articulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Articulation "Skyrim:Amulet of Articulation"), Enthir can be persuaded to just return the amulet.
- Onmund's Amulet might be a different material, depending on the level you do this quest: such as a plain gold necklace, a silver emerald necklace, etc.
- It is possible to keep the Grand Staff of Charming for yourself by placing it on a weapon rack before returning to Enthir to trade it in for Onmund's Amulet. After obtaining the amulet, you can safely retrieve the staff from the weapon rack and do as you please with it.
- Unlike a few other (not College of Winterhold affiliated) quests which NPCs ask you to retrieve jewelry, you cannot take back Onmund's Amulet from him once you turn it in, via any means (pickpocketing, etc.). It vanishes from the game as soon as you hand it over to him.

## Bugs

- You cannot speak to Enthir about the quest if [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") quest is active.
- If the staff is found before starting the quest, it will have weight, and cannot be removed from your inventory. The quest will not show an icon on the map and dialogue options are not available to return the staff to Enthir. To fix these issues, equip the staff, and activate a weapon rack. An icon will then appear, hinting to pick up the staff. Picking up the staff will update the quest journal, directing you to return the staff to Enthir.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  - This does not always work on Xbox One; even using the weapon rack trick will not fix the problem.
  -  The console command `setstage MGRAppOnmund01 30` will allow you to advance. Also, if you successfully persuade Enthir to give back the amulet and complete the quest, the staff is no longer considered a quest item and can be dropped/stored/sold normally.
  - If the quest has been taken, equip the staff, open console and type `player.drop 00029B91 1`. The staff will be dropped, and the quest continues as normal.

## Quest Stages

| 30 |  | I have found the staff that Enthir wanted, and need to deliver it to him so that he'll exchange it for Onmund's amulet. *Objective 30:* Deliver the staff to Enthir |
| 40 |  | Enthir agreed to return Onmund's amulet to him, and has given it to me. I need to make sure it gets back to Onmund. *Objective 40:* Deliver the amulet to Onmund |
| 200 | ☑ | Onmund is grateful that I was able to deal with Enthir and return his amulet. |
| 255 | ☒ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGRAppOnmund01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGRAppOnmund01`.

# Skyrim:Orc Strongholds

## Overview

Dushnikh Yal

 This page lists all the **Orc strongholds** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:    **[Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal")** — A prosperous Orc stronghold in the southwest of Skyrim, southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dushnikh+Yal)
:    **[Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur")** — An accursed Orc stronghold beset by giants in the southeast of Skyrim, west-southwest of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Largashbur)
:    **[Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur")** — An Orc stronghold in the far northwest of Skyrim, west of Solitude and north of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur)
:    **[Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur")** — An Orc stronghold in the east of Skyrim, southeast of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Narzulbur)

## Blood-Kin

Only [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") characters have immediate access to the strongholds unchallenged. Characters of any other race must first become [Blood-Kin of the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin_of_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Blood-Kin of the Orcs") before being welcome in the strongholds. You can enter a stronghold without being Blood-Kin, but the residents will continuously tell you that you are not welcome. If the stronghold includes [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants"), [trainers](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers"), or potential [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), their services will be unavailable until you comply.

Several quests fulfill this requirement. Members of any stronghold you approach may give you the quest [The Forgemaster's Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forgemaster%27s_Fingers "Skyrim:The Forgemaster's Fingers") if you have not become Blood-Kin already. Alternatively, completing any quest listed below will make you Blood-Kin. Upon first completing one of these quests, the grateful Orc will say, *"For your help, I'm sending word to the Orc strongholds that you're to be trusted. You should be welcome there now."*, signifying that you are now Blood-Kin. In addition, each associated Orc's [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you will increase by 1 upon completing the quests below, with two possible exceptions.

| Quest | Location | Grateful Orc |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Coated in Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Coated_in_Blood "Skyrim:Coated in Blood") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol") |
| [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe") | [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") | [Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob") |
| [Fetch me that Book!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fetch_me_that_Book! "Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!") | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") | [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") |
| [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)") | [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine") | [Gat gro-Shargakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gat_gro-Shargakh "Skyrim:Gat gro-Shargakh") |
| [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)") [†](#intnote_Sanuarach_Mine) | [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") | [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh") |
| [Skilled Apprenticeship](/wiki/Skyrim:Skilled_Apprenticeship "Skyrim:Skilled Apprenticeship") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") |
| [Mine Ore (Iron)](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") | [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") | [Grogmar gro-Burzag](/wiki/Skyrim:Grogmar_gro-Burzag "Skyrim:Grogmar gro-Burzag") |
| [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") [DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") [†](#intnote_Prophet) | [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") [DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") [DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |

[†](#note_Sanuarach_Mine)You must convince Atar to leave Sanuarach Mine to impress Lash gra-Dushnikh.

[†](#note_Prophet)You must finish the Dawnguard version of this quest to impress Durak.

## Notes

- If you start "[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")" as an Orc, [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") will say: *"You from one of the strongholds, Orc? How did you end up here?"*
- If you become Blood-Kin and later bring your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to the Orc strongholds, the residents will treat your follower as an extra ally as long as you and your follower are together.
- Another Orc who would've made you Blood-Kin, named [Makhel Abbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Makhel_Abbas "Skyrim:Makhel Abbas"), was meant to play a role in a Civil War quest, but this quest didn't make it into the final game.

## Bugs

- [Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub") and [Garakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Garakh "Skyrim:Garakh") at [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") were apparently intended to be merchants (apothecary and blacksmith respectively), but do not function as merchants themselves.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. They were assigned the wrong settings. Once fixed, they will be affected by [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader"), but not [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor").
- Even after becoming Blood-Kin to the Orcs, you may still be warned about trespassing in the longhouses at the Orc strongholds.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Orc Strongholds

## Overview

Dushnikh Yal

 This page lists all the **Orc strongholds** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:    **[Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal")** — A prosperous Orc stronghold in the southwest of Skyrim, southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dushnikh+Yal)
:    **[Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur")** — An accursed Orc stronghold beset by giants in the southeast of Skyrim, west-southwest of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Largashbur)
:    **[Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur")** — An Orc stronghold in the far northwest of Skyrim, west of Solitude and north of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur)
:    **[Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur")** — An Orc stronghold in the east of Skyrim, southeast of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Narzulbur)

## Blood-Kin

Only [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") characters have immediate access to the strongholds unchallenged. Characters of any other race must first become [Blood-Kin of the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin_of_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Blood-Kin of the Orcs") before being welcome in the strongholds. You can enter a stronghold without being Blood-Kin, but the residents will continuously tell you that you are not welcome. If the stronghold includes [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants"), [trainers](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers"), or potential [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), their services will be unavailable until you comply.

Several quests fulfill this requirement. Members of any stronghold you approach may give you the quest [The Forgemaster's Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forgemaster%27s_Fingers "Skyrim:The Forgemaster's Fingers") if you have not become Blood-Kin already. Alternatively, completing any quest listed below will make you Blood-Kin. Upon first completing one of these quests, the grateful Orc will say, *"For your help, I'm sending word to the Orc strongholds that you're to be trusted. You should be welcome there now."*, signifying that you are now Blood-Kin. In addition, each associated Orc's [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") towards you will increase by 1 upon completing the quests below, with two possible exceptions.

| Quest | Location | Grateful Orc |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Coated in Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Coated_in_Blood "Skyrim:Coated in Blood") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Moth gro-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Moth_gro-Bagol "Skyrim:Moth gro-Bagol") |
| [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe") | [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") | [Gularzob](/wiki/Skyrim:Gularzob "Skyrim:Gularzob") |
| [Fetch me that Book!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fetch_me_that_Book! "Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!") | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") | [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") |
| [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)") | [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine") | [Gat gro-Shargakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gat_gro-Shargakh "Skyrim:Gat gro-Shargakh") |
| [Sanuarach Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanuarach_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Sanuarach Mine (quest)") [†](#intnote_Sanuarach_Mine) | [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") | [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh") |
| [Skilled Apprenticeship](/wiki/Skyrim:Skilled_Apprenticeship "Skyrim:Skilled Apprenticeship") | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") |
| [Mine Ore (Iron)](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") | [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") | [Grogmar gro-Burzag](/wiki/Skyrim:Grogmar_gro-Burzag "Skyrim:Grogmar gro-Burzag") |
| [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") [DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") [†](#intnote_Prophet) | [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") [DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | [Durak](/wiki/Skyrim:Durak "Skyrim:Durak") [DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |

[†](#note_Sanuarach_Mine)You must convince Atar to leave Sanuarach Mine to impress Lash gra-Dushnikh.

[†](#note_Prophet)You must finish the Dawnguard version of this quest to impress Durak.

## Notes

- If you start "[Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound")" as an Orc, [Hadvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hadvar "Skyrim:Hadvar") will say: *"You from one of the strongholds, Orc? How did you end up here?"*
- If you become Blood-Kin and later bring your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") to the Orc strongholds, the residents will treat your follower as an extra ally as long as you and your follower are together.
- Another Orc who would've made you Blood-Kin, named [Makhel Abbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Makhel_Abbas "Skyrim:Makhel Abbas"), was meant to play a role in a Civil War quest, but this quest didn't make it into the final game.

## Bugs

- [Atub](/wiki/Skyrim:Atub "Skyrim:Atub") and [Garakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Garakh "Skyrim:Garakh") at [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") were apparently intended to be merchants (apothecary and blacksmith respectively), but do not function as merchants themselves.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. They were assigned the wrong settings. Once fixed, they will be affected by [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader"), but not [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor").
- Even after becoming Blood-Kin to the Orcs, you may still be warned about trespassing in the longhouses at the Orc strongholds.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Orotheim

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Orotheim ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orotheim)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Mace Etiquette](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_Etiquette "Skyrim:Mace Etiquette")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| Orotheim01 | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| Northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") Southeast of [Robber's Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Robber%27s_Gorge "Skyrim:Robber's Gorge") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |
| # of [Forges/Anvils](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") | 1 |

| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Orotheim

**Orotheim** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") that is home to bandits intent on poaching [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"). There is only one zone to the cave, *[Orotheim](#Orotheim)*.

The cave is northeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"), past [Talking Stone Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Talking_Stone_Camp "Skyrim:Talking Stone Camp"), on the cliffs above [Crabber's Shanty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crabber%27s_Shanty "Skyrim:Crabber's Shanty").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers.
- **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad").
- **[Stealing Plans](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealing_Plans "Skyrim:Stealing Plans")**: Search a Silver Hand hideout for information on the location of their headquarters.
- **[Striking the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Striking_the_Heart "Skyrim:Striking the Heart")**: Assassinate a leader of the Silver Hand.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There is a rough path running northwest from the [River Hjaal](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Hjaal "Skyrim:River Hjaal"), that curls around the edge of the mountain to the entrance. There are a number of [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") in the undergrowth around the cave and grisly stakes with corpses speared through their stomachs either side of the entrance. There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") among the rocks above the entrance to the cave.

### Orotheim

The cave is split into three rough rooms. Just behind where you enter there is a [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") plant, then along the walls of the tunnel there are several types of fungi: three [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungi, a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus, an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), and a [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), as well as another lavender. The first room is inhabited by two [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), one on the ground level, and another on the wooden platform above, usually using the smithing equipment. Around the edges of the room are four imp stool, two fly amanita, a bleeding crown and a Namira's rot fungi. There is a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") above the campfire, and a [mammoth snout](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Snout "Skyrim:Mammoth Snout") and two [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") are on the table. There is also a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") in the middle of the room.

On the platform there is a table with some [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). To the right are some boxes and sacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), on top of which is a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mace Etiquette](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_Etiquette "Skyrim:Mace Etiquette")*. Past that there are an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a weapon rack with an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"). There is a ledge to the right of the grindstone where two imp stools and two bleeding crowns are growing. Along the short tunnel to the next room there are two imp stool fungi, two fly amanita fungi, and a lavender plant. On the ledge high up on the right of the tunnel, another fly amanita, and a [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") are growing.

The tunnel opens on a wooden platform where a bandit alternates between leaning on a table to the left, and using a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). Two bandits are located in the lower part of the room, one of whom is the bandit leader. The bandit leader carries a [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit%27s_Journal_(Orotheim) "Skyrim:Bandit's Journal (Orotheim)") describing the reason behind setting up camp in the cave. Around the campfire are four hay piles. By the wooden platform is a table with two chairs and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and behind that, under the platform, are a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and an apprentice-locked chest. Around the room are a lot more patches of fungi; there are five imp stool, four bleeding crown, three fly amanita, two blisterwort, and a Namira's rot.

Through the tunnel to the southwest, where a rather pointless [bone chime](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hangs, is the treasure room. To the right is a table with a leveled weapon, an iron war axe, a satchel, a coin purse, a random potion, and several bottles of wine and ale. Straight ahead is an unlocked chest. Opposite the chest is a stack of crates with a random pair of boots among them. To the south is a torch, and to the right of that is a pull chain that lowers a portion of the wall above the very first room. Through the treasure room and the ledge above the first room are more [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"): three imp stool, two fly amanita, and two Namira's rot.

## Notes

- While Orotheim does not have a large amount of a single fungus or plant, it does have a large amount of alchemical ingredients in total, especially considering its relative size. It includes 17 imp stool, 13 fly amanita, 8 bleeding crown, 5 Namira's rot, 3 lavender, 2 blisterwort, and 1 white cap.
- Due west, below the second waterfall on the river, is a skeleton lying next to a novice-locked chest. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-70488&y=37584&zoom=17&legacy=true)

## Bugs

- The iron ore vein above the entrance may not be able to be interacted with **?**

# Skyrim:Orphan Rock

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Orphan Rock ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan+Rock)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| Occupants | |
| [Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") or [Hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), [Hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Nettlebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| OrphanRockExterior01, OrphanRockExterior02, OrphanRockExterior03 | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| Northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") South of [North Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:North Skybound Watch") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |

Orphan Rock

**Orphan Rock** is a wooded valley with a central rock plateau northeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch") or [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") led by a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").

This location shows no sign of habitation and the rock plateau is not easily accessible until you are sent to retrieve [Nettlebane](/wiki/Skyrim:Nettlebane "Skyrim:Nettlebane") during the quest [The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature").

## Related Quests

- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

## Walkthrough

The path leading up to the rock runs north from the road between Helgen and [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). Caution is advised when exploring the area, as four [elemental rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Rune "Skyrim:Elemental Rune") traps, two [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap"), and two sets of sharpened stakes similar to those at the bottom of a [spike pit](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Pit "Skyrim:Spike Pit") trap are in the vicinity. A [dead bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead) "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") is near one of the sets of sharpened stakes. Many [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a few patches of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus grow nearby. As you approach from the south, an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is behind a dead tree stump to the west. Farther north is a fallen tree next to a spike with wolf heads on it. The western end of the tree is hollow, with a lootable skeleton next to a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") inside.

The first tent

Two witches or hags are on the valley floor, and another two rest near the tent by the path at the top of the slope. All four will attack on sight using low-level [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells and [daggers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). The large central rock is accessed by crossing a fallen tree trunk over a small chasm near the tent. The plateau is guarded by a single hagraven wielding more powerful fire spells. It is possible to fight the first pair of witches or hags without alarming the pair on the upper level and the hagraven.

On the near side of the fallen tree, a tent to the right contains two unowned bedrolls, an adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Fruit.2FVegetables "Skyrim:Food") sack. To the right of the tent are several barrels and sacks, most of which contain food, though one barrel contains [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and has a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") on top. In front of these is a campfire and a wooden table holding a skeleton that can be looted for a few [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

The hagraven

The most notable loot is Nettlebane, found on the body of the hagraven. A chest and an unowned hay pile are in the hagraven's tent on the central rock. To the left of the tent is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") holding a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flower, a [hagraven claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), and a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"). In front of the enchanter is a large bowl on a stand with the body of a dead [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") lying on top; this can be harvested for a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"). A [silverside perch](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverside_Perch "Skyrim:Silverside Perch") and a [river betty](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Betty "Skyrim:River Betty") lie on a rock among some blood splatters in front of the tent.

## Notes

- A [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") is to the north-northeast, toward [North Skybound Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:North_Skybound_Watch "Skyrim:North Skybound Watch").
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map displays what the area looks like before the quest; the previous one displayed what the area looks like after the quest begins.

## Bugs

- Southeast of the hagraven's tent, past the dead spriggan, are two rubies suspended in the air over the peak of a rock.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.5, addresses this issue. The rubies have been placed on the arcane enchanter.

# Skyrim:Orphan's Tear

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shipwreck.png) | Shipwreck: Orphan's Tear ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan%27s+Tear)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| OrphansTearExterior, OrphansTearExterior02 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| West of [Ravenscar Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hollow "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") | 1 |

Orphan's Tear

**Orphan's Tear** is a [shipwreck](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") west of [Ravenscar Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hollow "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow") on the northern coast.

The ship has broken into two sections; one section is partially submerged and holds the cabin, while the other is almost fully submerged. It is occupied by three [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

## Related Quests

- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Orphan's Tear bandit camp

There are three bandits based here, who will become hostile and attack as soon as you approach. They are a melee fighter, an archer, and a magic user. Once they are taken care of, you can proceed with exploring the shipwreck. The bandits' campsite on the shore consists of a campfire and a large tent with two bedrolls and a table holding some cheese wedges and a wheel, and an adept-locked chest containing random [leveled loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") just outside the tent. Near the tent, there are four [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging from a rack and a bucket containing three more salmon behind a small boat, all of which can be harvested. Beside the bucket of salmon are some crates with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") creation installed, there is also a fishing pole here, with some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") found a bit farther up the shore. Fish that can be found in freezing waters can be found here. There is also a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") lying on a wooden block in front of the large tent.

Inside the shipwreck's cabin, you will see a table propped up against the wall with an unlocked chest hidden behind it. Also, if you look hard enough, you can find two bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") and a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") beside the bedroll. There are a couple of barrels on this level containing foodstuffs. Proceed down the stairs into the water to find several barrels containing common [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") and also a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") near a bed. If you proceed farther down one level you will see a skeleton trapped underwater to the left of the stairs, along with another unlocked chest surrounded by four barrels. To the right of the stairs is a [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka").

There are two harvestable clams between the two parts of the boat and two [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") plants next to the large tent. The other submerged section of the shipwreck does not have any notable loot, however, other than a few barrels.

## Notes

- There is a total of 45 [Nordic barnacle clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle_Cluster "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle Cluster") in the area, where you can harvest [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle").
- There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") southeast of the campsite.
