# Skyrim:Oslaf's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Oslaf's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Oslaf%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2SVOslafsHouse | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Oslaf's House

**Oslaf's House** is the home of [Oslaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf "Skyrim:Oslaf"), [Finna](/wiki/Skyrim:Finna "Skyrim:Finna"), and their daughter [Aeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeta "Skyrim:Aeta") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

It is on the southwest side of the village, between [Deor Woodcutter's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter%27s_House "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter's House") to the southeast and [Wulf Wild-Blood's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood%27s_House "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood's House") to the north.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Aeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Aeta "Skyrim:Aeta")  [Finna](/wiki/Skyrim:Finna "Skyrim:Finna")  [Oslaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf "Skyrim:Oslaf") |

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance is an empty cart. Along the east wall is the entrance to a pen holding two [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"). Behind the house is a small vegetable plot containing two [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), five [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), four [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and six [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), with two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") in and near the goat pen. To the right of the entrance is a crate and two fish barrels. The entrance has a novice lock.

### Oslaf's House

Home cooking

The entrance leads into a small room with a fire pit in the center and a rack holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), two [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") samples, and two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids. Beside the fire pit is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") on a stand. On your right against the east wall is a sideboard with a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top. In the northeast corner is a small round table and two chairs. On the north wall are four shelves containing a loaf of bread, three [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a leek and a cast iron pot containing a cabbage. In the northwest corner is a set of shelves containing a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), three bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and two sacks. Against the west wall on a ledge are two more sacks. Three small steps lead up to the south into the main part of the house.

Cozy living

In the next room there is a wall shelf on your left with a goat cheese wheel, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and two [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"). On your right is a sack and in the northwest corner another small round table and three chairs. On the table is a bowl of [beef stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Beef_Stew "Skyrim:Beef Stew") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Above the table on the north wall are two wall shelves containing three potatoes, a bottle of wine and a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"). In the southwest corner is a cupboard and on the shelves are two potatoes, a cabbage and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and on top of the cupboard is a sack. There is a narrow table against the south wall with two sacks underneath. Leading up to the upstairs is a flight of stairs against the east wall, with a doorway underneath, this leads to Aeta's bedroom that has a small square table and two chairs in front of you, with a [Horker loaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Loaf "Skyrim:Horker Loaf") on a plate on the table and against the north wall a single bed with an end table has a copy of *[Words of the Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_of_the_Wind "Skyrim:Words of the Wind")* and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") on top.

Climbing the stairs, there is an end table in the southeast corner with a low table and two chairs to the left. On the table is a copy of *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*. To your left is a doorway into Oslaf and Finna's bedroom. As you enter there is a wardrobe on your left against the south wall with a chair next to it. In the northwest corner is an end table with a wooden bowl containing a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") on top. A double bed is to the right of it coming out from the north wall. Beside the bed against the east wall is an open crate with three pairs of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") in. Finally in the southeast corner is a small round table with a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") on top.

# Skyrim:Other Places

## Overview

Frostflow Lighthouse

This page lists **other miscellaneous places** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

## Docks

:    **[East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse")** — A warehouse on the Solitude docks immediately southeast of the city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=East+Empire+Company+Warehouse)
:    **[Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small isolated dock far west of Solitude and northwest of Northwatch Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Icewater+Jetty+%28DG%29)
:    **[Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small abandoned dock on the northwest coast of Solstheim inhabited by mudcrabs. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Northshore+Landing)
:    **[Riften Docks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Docks "Skyrim:Riften Docks")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") — An extensive dock located on the western side of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Riften+Docks+%28CC%29)

## Lighthouses

:    **[Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse")** — A lighthouse west-southwest of Winterhold containing Falmer, chaurus, and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostflow+Lighthouse)
:    **[Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse")** — A stone building on the northern coast of Skyrim that helps to guide ships into Solitude harbor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Lighthouse)

## Libraries

:   **[The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum")** — The library located within the College of Winterhold, zealously maintained by Urag gro-Shub. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Arcanaeum)

## Cellars

*For other uses, see [Cellar (disambiguation)](/wiki/Skyrim:Cellar_(disambiguation) "Skyrim:Cellar (disambiguation)").*

:   **[Burguk's Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Cellar_(Burguk%27s_Longhouse) "Skyrim:Cellar (Burguk's Longhouse)")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Dushnikh Yal inside the Dushnikh Yal Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Cellar)
:   **[Ironback Hideout Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Crossbows "Skyrim:Elite Crossbows") — A cellar located underneath the ruined house at Ironback Hideout. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironback+Hideout+Cellar)
:   **[Largashbur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Cellar "Skyrim:Largashbur Cellar")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Largashbur behind the Largashbur Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Largashbur+Cellar)
:   **[Mauhulakh's Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mauhulakh%27s_Cellar "Skyrim:Mauhulakh's Cellar")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Nazulbur in the front of Nazulbur Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Mauhulakh%27s+Cellar)
:   **[Mor Khazgur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Cellar "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Cellar")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Mor Khazgur behind the Mor Khazgur Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur+Cellar)
:   **[Old Attius Farm Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm_Cellar "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm Cellar")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") — A cellar located underneath the ruined house at Old Attius Farm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Old+Attius+Farm+Cellar+%28CC%29)

## Root Tunnels

:   **[Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") — A sewer system located in western Solitude, overrun with Sheogorath's influence. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-62548&y=106269&zoom=17)

## Ayleid Ruins

:   **[Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") — A medium-sized Ayleid ruin located beneath the Jerall Mountains, just east of the Pale Pass. It straddles the border between the Rift in Skyrim and County Bruma in Cyrodiil. In Skyrim, it is accessed from the north by way of Varlais Cavern, a cave entrance located to the south of Arcwind Point. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rielle+%28CC%29)

# Skyrim:Other Places

## Overview

Frostflow Lighthouse

This page lists **other miscellaneous places** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

## Docks

:    **[East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse")** — A warehouse on the Solitude docks immediately southeast of the city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=East+Empire+Company+Warehouse)
:    **[Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small isolated dock far west of Solitude and northwest of Northwatch Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Icewater+Jetty+%28DG%29)
:    **[Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small abandoned dock on the northwest coast of Solstheim inhabited by mudcrabs. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Northshore+Landing)
:    **[Riften Docks](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Docks "Skyrim:Riften Docks")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") — An extensive dock located on the western side of Riften. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Riften+Docks+%28CC%29)

## Lighthouses

:    **[Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse")** — A lighthouse west-southwest of Winterhold containing Falmer, chaurus, and frostbite spiders. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostflow+Lighthouse)
:    **[Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse")** — A stone building on the northern coast of Skyrim that helps to guide ships into Solitude harbor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Lighthouse)

## Libraries

:   **[The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum")** — The library located within the College of Winterhold, zealously maintained by Urag gro-Shub. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Arcanaeum)

## Cellars

*For other uses, see [Cellar (disambiguation)](/wiki/Skyrim:Cellar_(disambiguation) "Skyrim:Cellar (disambiguation)").*

:   **[Burguk's Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Cellar_(Burguk%27s_Longhouse) "Skyrim:Cellar (Burguk's Longhouse)")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Dushnikh Yal inside the Dushnikh Yal Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Cellar)
:   **[Ironback Hideout Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout_Cellar "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout Cellar")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Crossbows "Skyrim:Elite Crossbows") — A cellar located underneath the ruined house at Ironback Hideout. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironback+Hideout+Cellar)
:   **[Largashbur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur_Cellar "Skyrim:Largashbur Cellar")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Largashbur behind the Largashbur Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Largashbur+Cellar)
:   **[Mauhulakh's Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mauhulakh%27s_Cellar "Skyrim:Mauhulakh's Cellar")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Nazulbur in the front of Nazulbur Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=Mauhulakh%27s+Cellar)
:   **[Mor Khazgur Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur_Cellar "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur Cellar")** — A cellar located in the Orc stronghold of Mor Khazgur behind the Mor Khazgur Longhouse. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mor+Khazgur+Cellar)
:   **[Old Attius Farm Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm_Cellar "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm Cellar")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal") — A cellar located underneath the ruined house at Old Attius Farm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Old+Attius+Farm+Cellar+%28CC%29)

## Root Tunnels

:   **[Solitude Sewers](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sewers "Skyrim:Solitude Sewers")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") — A sewer system located in western Solitude, overrun with Sheogorath's influence. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-62548&y=106269&zoom=17)

## Ayleid Ruins

:   **[Rielle](/wiki/Skyrim:Rielle "Skyrim:Rielle")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause") — A medium-sized Ayleid ruin located beneath the Jerall Mountains, just east of the Pale Pass. It straddles the border between the Rift in Skyrim and County Bruma in Cyrodiil. In Skyrim, it is accessed from the north by way of Varlais Cavern, a cave entrance located to the south of Arcwind Point. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rielle+%28CC%29)

# Skyrim:Out of Balance

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Purify the focus points for magical energy around the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"),  [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance") |
| Reward: | Soul gems, temporary [Regenerate Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka") effect (see [bugs](#Bugs) section) |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 (Drevis) |
| ID: | MGR02 |

The focal point in the center courtyard of the College of Winterhold

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to each of the focal points around the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
2. Activate them with the [Mystic Tuning Gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystic_Tuning_Gloves "Skyrim:Mystic Tuning Gloves") equipped.
3. Return to [Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren").

### Fine Tuning

[Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren") can be found in the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance") at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). Ask him if there is any College business that you can assist with and he will answer, *"There may be a matter in which your... skills... could be useful. The various points of focus for magic energies around the College have become polluted, and need cleansing. The magical energies underneath the college still require purification. Your assistance would be most useful."* When you agree to help, Drevis will provide you with the [mystic tuning gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystic_Tuning_Gloves "Skyrim:Mystic Tuning Gloves") and let you know what needs to be done: *"...These specially enchanted gloves will allow you to delve directly into the focal points for these energies. Go to each focal point and remove whatever impurities you may find there. Return the gloves to me when you have finished. Please exercise caution. This is not a procedure without possible... consequences."*

### Purification

The three magical focal points associated with this quest are the large, blue, fountains of energy found around the College. One is outside in the main College courtyard, one in the Hall of Countenance and another in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). In order to begin equip the mystic tuning gloves to receive the Activate Mystic Focal Point prompt when you approach each font. Despite Drevis' warning, the purification process is quite simple with no real consequence associated.

### Reward

Once all three focal points have been purified, return to Drevis. When you tell him that the focal points have been cleansed, he will respond *"Yes, they have. I can feel the difference already. But of course, I'm far more in tune with these sorts of things than most. Thank you. I appreciate your assistance."* Your reward for completion of each location is random [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and/or temporary [Regenerate Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka") effects (see [bugs](#Bugs) section).

## Notes

- Drevis is meant to give you the quest more than once if you talk to him again later, but due to erroneous scripting, this does not always happen.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12181))
- Based on the game data, it appears that five points were originally intended, but only three were implemented in the final game. One of the additional points would have been a pillar at the base of the first ramp coming down from the college; the other one has no location assigned. In addition, one of the possible effects would have been to spawn a creature, however this is also unimplemented.
- It is possible to save scum each focal point into yielding a grand soul gem.
- You can usually cleanse a focal point twice by clicking the activate key/button repeatedly, for two rewards at each location.
- You can pickpocket the Mystic Tuning Gloves off of Neloren immediately after finishing the quest. However, they will be marked as quest items if you do so, meaning that it will be impossible to remove them from your inventory afterwards.

## Bugs

- When cleansing the foci, either or both of two different bugged two-hour boosts to magicka regeneration may be placed on you. In your Active Effects list, they appear as "Fortify Magicka"; one with a nominal drain effect, the other with a nominal fortify effect. These boosts appear to stack. Some players have reported that they remain much longer than two hours.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
  -  If you installed Dawnguard, you can use `dispelallspells` to dispel all active effects on you except enchanted equipment.
- The magicka regeneration may actually give you unlimited magicka for a time.
- A dragon attack on the College of Winterhold may disrupt this quest and not register the foci as cleansed. Simply kill the dragon and return to all focal points and reactivate as necessary. **?**
- The gloves may not appear in your inventory, even with attempts to add them using console commands.

## Quest Stages

| Out of Balance (MGR02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Drevis Neloren has asked for my help in purifying the focus points for magical energy around the College. I've been given special Tuning gloves that I'll need to wear in order to cleanse the focal points. Drevis has warned that there may be side-effects to performing this task. *Objective 10:* Cleanse the focal points for magical energies around the College |
| 20 |  | I've finished cleansing the focal points around the College, and should take the gloves back to Drevis. *Objective 20:* Return to Drevis Neloren |
| 200 | ☑ | I've successfully helped Drevis by cleansing the focal points around the College. |
| 255 | ☒ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGR02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGR02`.

# Skyrim:Over the Edge

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **A criminal has sensed his past catching up with him.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Added after reading the note *[Suicide at Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Suicide_at_Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Suicide at Dragon Bridge")* |
| Location(s): | [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") |
| Reward: | Set of [enchanted steel soldier armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier_Items "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier Items"), ability to craft [steel soldier armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel#Steel_Soldier_Armor "Skyrim:Steel") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE058\_Quest, ccBGSSSE058\_MiscQuest |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier") |

The suicide

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Look for a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Suicide_at_Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Suicide at Dragon Bridge") at the Four Shields Tavern.
2. Search downriver for the [body](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_(Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier) "Skyrim:Guard (Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier)").
3. Read [the guard's note](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Note_on_Aldepius "Skyrim:Guard's Note on Aldepius").
4. Confront [Aldepius](/wiki/Skyrim:Aldepius "Skyrim:Aldepius").
5. Meet [Peladius](/wiki/Skyrim:Peladius "Skyrim:Peladius") on the Dragon Bridge.
6. Defeat Peladius.
7. Retrieve the armor.

### A Suicide in Haafingar

Upon installing the [Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), you will be directed to read a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Suicide_at_Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Suicide at Dragon Bridge") located in the [Four Shields Tavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Shields_Tavern "Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern") in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). Reading it, you will learn of an apparent suicide which took place at the town's eponymous Dragon Bridge. A new recruit guardsman had gone missing but a fellow guard named [Aldepius](/wiki/Skyrim:Aldepius "Skyrim:Aldepius") claims to have seen him leap from the bridge.

You will find the [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_(Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier) "Skyrim:Guard (Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier)")'s body quite a ways downstream to the northeast of the bridge (though on the south bank of the river). It is just before the river meets another on their way to the bay at Solitude; about half-way between Dragon Bridge and the Solitude Sawmill. On the guard's body, you will find [a note](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard%27s_Note_on_Aldepius "Skyrim:Guard's Note on Aldepius") that shows the dead guard suspected Aldepius of being a bandit informant rather than a stationed member of the Dragon Bridge garrison. You will need to return to town to confront Aldepius.

### Duel at the Dragon Bridge

Face Peladius on the bridge

Upon re-entering the Four Shields Tavern, you will find that Aldepius is nowhere to be found. Instead, he has left a [confession](/wiki/Skyrim:Aldepius%27_Confession "Skyrim:Aldepius' Confession") at one of the tables, inviting you to face him in honorable combat at the Dragon Bridge. In it he admits that his real name is [Peladius](/wiki/Skyrim:Peladius "Skyrim:Peladius") and that he is a former member of the [Crimson Dirks](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Dirks "Skyrim:Crimson Dirks") bandit gang.

Peladius will be waiting for you on the bridge and will attack on sight, so be prepared to fight to the death. Grant him the honorable death he wishes for, and loot his body for a full set of [enchanted steel soldier armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier_Items "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier Items"). This will complete the quest and will grant you the ability to craft this new armor for yourself.

## Notes

- If the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") still holds [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), the guards involved in this quest will be wearing Solitude colors. If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") have taken the city, the guards will be wearing Stormcloak armor instead.

It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE058_Quest, ccBGSSSE058_MiscQuest`.

# Skyrim:Paarthurnax (quest)

## Overview

This article is about the quest. For the dragon, see [Paarthurnax (dragon)](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Main.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Main.png) | **Deal with a [potential threat](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") or [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") |
| Location(s): | [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") |
| Reward: | Free access to Sky Haven Temple restored |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =3 ([Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine"))   =3 ([Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern"))   =-2 ([Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir")) |
| ID: | MQPaarthurnax |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") | | |

.jpg)

Paarthurnax in combat

## Quick Walkthrough

1. (Optional) Talk to [Esbern](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern "Skyrim:Esbern") or [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine").
2. Kill [Paarthurnax](/wiki/Skyrim:Paarthurnax_(dragon) "Skyrim:Paarthurnax (dragon)").
3. Return to Esbern or Delphine.
4. Tell them Paarthurnax is dead.

### Initiating the Quest

This quest may initiate in two ways:

- **At your discretion:** After you complete [Alduin's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Alduin's Bane") and defeat the World-Eater in combat, you may consult with Esbern to learn of [Alduin's](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin") whereabouts. This begins the quest.
- **Automatically:** If you have not yet spoken with Esbern or Delphine at [Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple"), when the [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") conference is held, Delphine will approach you and start the quest automatically. Delphine does require you to give a reply. She issues a demand and says you two have nothing to talk about until you have carried out the deed, even though talking to her is still possible.

### The Stakeholders

Delphine and Esbern have discovered that Paarthurnax is the Master of the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards") and an ancient enemy of the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades"). You can argue in Paarthurnax's defense, but both will reiterate the war crimes and atrocities committed by Paarthurnax. They will also claim that Paarthurnax helped Alduin enslave mortal ancestors and committed atrocities that were so severe, they are still remembered thousands of years later. In addition, Delphine thinks that Paarthurnax's betrayal of Alduin actually makes him worse, because it could mean that he might betray the Dragonborn in turn. They will tell you that their oaths as Blades prevents them from giving you any further help until you kill Paarthurnax.

If you go to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar") and tell [Arngeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Arngeir "Skyrim:Arngeir") that the Blades want Paarthurnax dead, he will tell you that Paarthurnax supported Alduin because all dragons were in league with Alduin at first, and that Paarthurnax could not help it. He will go on to say that Paarthurnax did eventually rebel against Alduin, and was instrumental in Alduin's first demise. You are given the option to tell him that Paarthurnax must die, that you are going to spare the dragon, or that you don't know what your decision will be. This will affect the conversation between Delphine and Arngeir if you are forced to negotiate a treaty in Season Unending.

Alternatively, you can go to Paarthurnax at [the Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:The Throat of the World") and talk to him there. He acknowledges that all dragons thirst for dominance and that the Dragonborn shares this thirst, though he believes that he has overcome this predisposition through the sheer power of will and that he can be trusted.

### The Choice

You do not need to give an explicit reply. If you choose not to carry out Delphine's order to kill Paarthurnax, the game withdraws this quest. It disappears from your quest log without any notice.

Paarthurnax is an easy foe for those who are leveled sufficiently, comparable to the average [Frost dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Dragon "Skyrim:Frost Dragon"). You will receive a dragon soul and the usual set of [dragon bones](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bone "Skyrim:Dragon Bone") and [dragon scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Scales "Skyrim:Dragon Scales") upon defeating him. Killing Paarthurnax will enrage Arngeir; if you return to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"), he will angrily lecture you on your decision and even go so far as to threaten violence if you do not leave. After this, the other Greybeards will also fail to acknowledge you. On the other hand, the Blades will talk to you again.

- **If Paarthurnax dies:**
  - Arngeir retracts the Greybeards' hospitality, and it is no longer possible to ask him for the locations of [word walls](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall").
  - Paarthurnax will no longer be around to provide meditation bonuses to certain [shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). If you already have a bonus, it will not go away; you will just be unable to change it.
  - Taking anything from High Hrothgar will count as stealing once again.
  - The Blades will welcome you once again and support you on Dragon Hunting missions.
  - An extra cutscene involving Paarthurnax after Alduin's defeat will be absent.
- **If Paarthurnax lives:**
  - Arngeir will still disclose the location of word walls.
  - Paarthurnax will still provide meditation bonuses for shout words.
  - Paarthurnax will appear for an extra cutscene after Alduin's defeat, wherein he details his plans to rein in the dragons and teach them to live peacefully, following the [Way of the Voice](/wiki/Lore:Way_of_the_Voice "Lore:Way of the Voice"). This does not make gameplay any different — some will attack, and some won't, unless you attack them. After this, the quest will disappear from the journal.
  - Taking anything from Sky Haven Temple will count as stealing.
  - Removing items from some containers in the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") will count as stealing, and you will lose access to the free bed there.
  - If you have not brought three people to the Blades already, Delphine's recruitment quest will remain uncompleted, or will become unavailable if you have not started it. However, it is entirely possible to recruit three followers for Delphine before being given the quest to kill Paarthurnax.
  - If you have not already obtained the [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Esbern%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Esbern's Potion") from [Esbern's Dragon Research](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Research "Skyrim:Dragon Research"), you will be unable to do so. In order to get the potion, you must do so between the quest [Alduin's Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin%27s_Wall "Skyrim:Alduin's Wall") and reading the Elder Scroll step of Alduin's Bane.
  - If you want the [Dragonslayer's Blessing](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonslayer%27s_Blessing "Skyrim:Dragonslayer's Blessing"), you'll be unable to get it. In order to get the blessing, you must do so between the quest Alduin's Wall and reading the Elder Scroll step of Alduin's Bane.
  - The only real consequence of *not* killing him is no longer having dialogue with both Delphine and Esbern, and thus no longer having the option to go on Dragon Hunts with your recruited Blades. They still, however, act like regular companions - but of course, can only accompany you one at a time, like any other companion, rather than all three at once on a specific dragon-hunt.

## Reward

The Blades do not reward you upon your return after killing Paarthurnax. Most of the gains come from the varied loot you find when searching Paarthurnax upon his death.

## Notes

- Because Delphine and Esbern are always essential characters and cannot die it is not possible to kill them to protect Paarthurnax. However, it is not necessary.
- While you can implicitly decline this quest and make it disappear from your active quests, you may still kill Paarthurnax at any later time. The quest will reappear in your journal and can be completed normally.
- If you accidentally killed Paarthurnax without creating a backup save but still want to talk to the Greybeards, try the following commands in the console and Arngeir will talk to you as if you were just back from killing Alduin:
  - `prid 3C57D resurrect` will resurrect Paarthurnax
  - `resetQuest MQPaarthurnax` will reset the quest that asked you to kill Paarthurnax
- If you speak to Arngeir after finishing the quest, he will be furious and say *"This is how you repay our trust? Paarthurnax's trust? His noble spirit... the wisdom of ages... his deep understanding of our existence... all gone, and for what? A mindless vendetta urged on you by a cabal of [Akaviri](/wiki/Lore:Akavir "Lore:Akavir") barbarians! Begone, before even my philosophy is tested beyond the breaking point. We are men of peace, and you are not."* Talking to Arngeir after that will cause him to only say *"We have nothing to say to each other. Paarthurnax's murder is beyond my powers of forgiveness."*

## Bugs

- It is unclear why, but Paarthurnax's health will sometimes regenerate, making it impossible to kill him. At what point in the game the regeneration begins and ends remains to be determined.
  - It is possible to bypass this bug by attacking Paarthurnax with [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes Razor").
  - Fast traveling away and back when Paarthurnax's health meter is empty may trigger Paarthurnax's death.
  - Ordering a follower to attack Paarthurnax may circumvent this bug.
- Often, Delphine will still allow you to recruit followers even after you have been told to kill Paarthurnax. Therefore, it is perfectly possible to complete that quest and not kill him.
- If you trigger the quest to kill Paarthurnax after completing [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)"), the quest will be permanently stuck in your journal unless you kill Paarthurnax.
- Even after killing Paarthurnax the miscellaneous quest "Talk to Esbern" may remain stuck in your journal.
- It is possible that after killing Paarthurnax, you will be unable to turn the quest in to Delphine, even though the quest arrow is pointing above her. If this happens, use the console to type: setstage MQPaarthurnax 100 **?**

## Quest Stages

| Paarthurnax (MQPaarthurnax) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | Delphine and Esbern have discovered that Paarthurnax was one of Alduin's chief allies during the ancient Dragon War. They refuse to give me any more help until I kill Paarthurnax. *Objective 10:* Kill Paarthurnax |
| 50 |  | Delphine and Esbern have discovered that Paarthurnax was one of Alduin's chief allies during the ancient Dragon War. I killed him, as they requested. *Objective 20:* Talk to Delphine |
| 100 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 15, 30, 150.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MQPaarthurnax stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MQPaarthurnax`.

# Skyrim:Paid in Full

## Overview

|  |  |

| [SR-qico-Thieves Guild.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Thieves_Guild.png) | **Recover the [bonemold formula](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Formula "Skyrim:Bonemold Formula") for [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") |
| Location(s): | [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"),  [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns"), [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") |
| Reward: | [Various Treasure](#The_Reward), [Exquisite Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Exquisite_Sapphire "Skyrim:Exquisite Sapphire") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory")) |
| ID: | DLC2TGQuest |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** Complete [Meet the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Meet_the_Family "Skyrim:Meet the Family") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | Complete [Meet the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Meet_the_Family "Skyrim:Meet the Family") | | |

A blacksmith with connections

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory").
2. Travel to [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns").
3. Recover the [bonemold formula](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Formula "Skyrim:Bonemold Formula") from [Esmond Tyne](/wiki/Skyrim:Esmond_Tyne "Skyrim:Esmond Tyne").
4. Give Glover the formula.
5. (*Optional*) Reveal the truth to an [old friend](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)").

### A Shadowmark in Raven Rock

*"So tell me... how's my brother Delvin?"*

For members of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") back in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), the local blacksmith of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") has a very familiar surname: Mallory. [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") has a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House") next to his smithy and to the left of the front door is a [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)"). Approach Glover when he is working the forge between 8am and 8pm and ask about the shadowmark. He will confess his relation to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") back in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), saying things like: *"So tell me... how's my brother Delvin? Still spending his nights at the Ragged Flagon trying to win Vex's heart?"* He will however also say: *"Damn layabout never even bothers to send his own flesh and blood a letter saying how he's doing. Can you imagine?"*

In the end, he will have a Thieves Guild-related job for you: *"Eager to make some coin, eh? That's the spirit. I'll tell you what. The Guild's got a problem out here that I've been trying to deal with for years, but haven't been able to handle. A fellow Breton who went by the name Esmond Tyne showed up on my doorstep about a fortnight ago. He noticed the shadowmarks like you did, and I thought he was one of us."* He will then proceed to tell you what [Esmond Tyne](/wiki/Skyrim:Esmond_Tyne "Skyrim:Esmond Tyne") stole: *"It's my own formula for improved bonemold. Took me years to perfect."* As for the whereabouts of Esmond, Glover only knows a bit: *"Well, before he ran off, he was talking some nonsense about trying to fence goods to the rieklings at Castle Karstaag. I told him he was crazy to even think about talking to those vicious little buggers, but he wouldn't listen. I'd bet a fat purse of coin that he's either dead or hiding out up there."* When you tell him you will retrieve the bonemold formula, he'll *"make sure you're set up right"*.

### Castle Karstaag Caverns

The remains of Esmond Tyne

[Castle Karstaag](/wiki/Lore:Castle_Karstaag "Lore:Castle Karstaag") is a massive fortress of ice, located in the northwestern region of Solstheim. Your objective is the  [Castle Karstaag Caverns](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Karstaag_Caverns "Skyrim:Castle Karstaag Caverns"), located at the bottom of the waterfall west of [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch"). Enter the Caverns and head upstream. [Rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") inhabit the cave and Esmond Tyne didn't make it very far in his attempt to fence goods to them. In the first huge chamber, he can be found dead with his lit lantern next to him. You can easily reach him by swimming silently, so you will never have to deal with the rieklings. Loot his corpse for the [bonemold formula](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Formula "Skyrim:Bonemold Formula") and various leveled loot and leave the Caverns the same way you came.

### The Reward

When you return to Glover with the formula in hand, he will not grieve over Esmond's death: *"I told him not to head up there. Sounds like the bloody fool got what he deserved."* He will then hand you the reward, the key to his house and basement, saying you can help yourself to whatever you find there. In fact, you can claim everything inside the house, so look around before heading down into the basement. Unlock the door and behold all the treasure, proving that Glover has been a high-esteemed Thieves Guild member and that he is very rich:

The hidden room

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| - [Thief Cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") - Strong Box - [Glover's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Glover's Letter") - Enchanted, leveled shield - Enchanted leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") - 3 [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") - 5 different [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Poisons "Skyrim:Potions") | - 3 different [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") - 4 coin purses - A complete set of [Blackguard's Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackguard%27s_Armor "Skyrim:Blackguard's Armor") - 3 bottles of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve") - 6 bottles of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") - [Lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") |

### One Last Thing

*"I... I can't believe it."*

Pick up [Glover's Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Glover's Letter") from the basement room and read through it. It solves the mystery about [Sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)") from [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") and reveals that Glover is her real father. It tells the tale about how he ran away from the farm where she was born, only to return fifteen years later when she had been abducted by bandits. It also reveals why Glover chose to move to Solstheim, simply because he saw her in the Thieves Guild and couldn't bear to tell her the truth.

Time to tell Sapphire the truth, so travel to Riften and seek out Sapphire. Hand her the letter and she will say: *"I... I can't believe it. All those years on the farm, and my mother never told me about any of this. Words can't even begin to describe how much I appreciate you bringing this to me. Here, take this. I used to carry it for good luck, but I think you deserve it more than I do."* She will then hand you an [exquisite sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Exquisite_Sapphire "Skyrim:Exquisite Sapphire"), a unique item worth 5000 gold.

## Notes

- You must be a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to do this quest.
- You need to have received your set of Thieves Guild armor from Tonilia in the Ragged Flagon, and you need to have asked both Vex and Delvin about extra work or read the book Shadowmarks by Delvin Mallory, to get the dialogue option to ask about the Shadowmark.
- The contents of Glover Mallory's house [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") after 10 days, making it possible to obtain several sets of the Blackguard's Armor.
- If you attempt to turn in the quest to Mallory before sunrise, he may be at the nearby Earth Stone. If so, he won't begin his scripted dialogue to finish the quest, and will only have his normal non-quest dialogue options if engaged in conversation. Wait until after daybreak to approach him and he will begin talking to you to complete the quest.

## Bugs

- If the bonemold formula was found before the quest was started, Glover Mallory never asks you to retrieve it and the quest cannot be started. **?**
  -  Open the console and type `setstage DLC2TGQuest 5`. You should be able to ask about the Thieves Guild problem and give him the formula once he mentions it.
- All the Blackguard's Armor items will respawn when Glover Mallory's basement resets, allowing multiple copies of the set to be obtained.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Glover's Letter respawns along with the rest of the house, allowing you to give it to Sapphire repeatedly and receive unlimited Exquisite Sapphires, since she is not coded to respond only once to it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch") fixes this bug.

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TGQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TGQuest`.

# Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor") |
| Location(s): | None |
| Reward: | 500 gold (per pendant) |
| ID: | DLC2RRFavor05 |

East Empire Company Strongbox

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
2. Find an [East Empire pendant](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant").
3. Bring the pendant to Fethis.

### East Empire Pendants

[Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor") runs a general goods outfit from [his house](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House "Skyrim:Alor House") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). You'll find that he is somewhat bitter about living and working in [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), should you speak with him. One thing that does seem to spark his interest is the [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant"). The pendants were once used as employee incentives, but are no longer being produced and, as a result, are now considered a valuable collector's item. Fethis lets you know that, if you find any of these East Empire pendants in your travels throughout Solstheim, he will be glad to buy them from you for 500 gold per pendant. The pendants are located in East Empire Company strongboxes, which are locked with an expert lock and contain other valuable loot as well.

### East Empire Company Strongbox Locations

There are 33 total locations of East Empire Company strongboxes in Solstheim, giving a profit of 16,500 gold if you can find them all. Most of the strongboxes are at locations marked on your map, but for those which are in [unmarked locations](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Dragonborn "Skyrim:Unmarked Places"), the entry for the "Location" column is the location from which it is easiest to find the strongbox. Certain strongboxes are marked as owned, which means taking from them is considered stealing, except in cases where you have raised the owner's [disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") high enough.

This is one of only two that isn't locked (see [bugs](#Bugs)). |
| Raven Rock [Northern Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Northern_Maiden "Skyrim:Northern Maiden") | [map](/wiki/File:SR-place-NorthernMaiden_StrongboxLocation.jpg "File:SR-place-NorthernMaiden StrongboxLocation.jpg") | Below the dock where the Northern Maiden waits in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), next to a [pearl oyster](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster"). |
| Raven Rock [Temple Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Temple Ancestral Tomb") | [map](/wiki/File:SR-place-TempleAncestralTomb_StrongboxLocation.jpg "File:SR-place-TempleAncestralTomb StrongboxLocation.jpg") | Northernmost alcove, sitting in the ash with the pile of bones. This is one of only two that isn't locked (see [bugs](#Bugs)). | [Clean Sweep](/wiki/Skyrim:Clean_Sweep "Skyrim:Clean Sweep"), [Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold") |
| Raven Rock [The Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark")[†](#intnote_stealing) | [map](/wiki/File:SR-place-Bulwark_StrongboxLocation.jpg "File:SR-place-Bulwark StrongboxLocation.jpg") | In the very back on the right, sitting in the northwest corner of the table. |

The strongbox is in the tent. You may be attacked by the rieklings who killed the elves. | [Lost Legacy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legacy "Skyrim:Lost Legacy") |
| [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") | [map](/wiki/File:SR-place-StridentSquall_StrongboxLocation.jpg "File:SR-place-StridentSquall StrongboxLocation.jpg") | On the bottom of a bookshelf on the southeast side in one of the lower decks. | [First Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:First_Edition "Skyrim:First Edition") |

[†](#note_stealing)This strongbox is marked as owned, which means taking from it is considered stealing.

## Notes

- The quest will not be completed or removed from the journal when the 33 pendants are turned in. It can only be removed from the journal by killing Fethis Alor or using the console. According to a note in the game data, this was done intentionally because the strongboxes are meant to respawn (however, they do not).
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.4, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12856)) It sets the strongboxes to respawn.
- To complete the quest using [console commands](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") `showqueststage dlc2rrfavor05` and some combination of `sets setstage (quest)` for the missing sequences of 20, 30, and 250; or `setobjectivecompleted dlc2rrfavor05 250 1`. The quest disappears from the log at quest stage 250.

## Bugs

- The strongboxes in Morvayn Manor Chambers and the Temple Ancestral Tomb are unlocked.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- The strongbox in The Retching Netch can be unlocked with the main Retching Netch key.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- One of the strongboxes in Raven Rock Mine can be unlocked with a version of Brand-Shei's Strongbox key that's unavailable in the game.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
  - If you have the [Wax Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Wax_Key "Skyrim:Wax Key") [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") perk and unlock this strongbox, the Brand-Shei's Strongbox key is given to you.

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 30, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RRFavor05 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RRFavor05`.

The Palace of the Kings in Windhelm

The **Palace of the Kings** is a large [castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") at the far end of the Valunstrad district in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It is home to the hold's [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl"), [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), and headquarters of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") movement.

There are four zones in the palace: *[Palace of the Kings](#Palace_of_the_Kings)*, *[Palace of the Kings Upstairs](#Palace_of_the_Kings_Upstairs)* (southern section), *[Palace of the Kings Upstairs](#POTKU2)* (northern section), and *[Windhelm Barracks](#Windhelm_Barracks)*. There is also a small [courtyard](#Courtyard) to the front of the palace.

The palace sits at the far end of Windhelm, on the opposite side of the city from the gates. There is an extra wall built between it and the city. Windhelm was one of the first human cities in [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel"), and also the capital of the first empire (which was founded by [Ysgramor](/wiki/Lore:Ysgramor "Lore:Ysgramor")). The palace is also one of the last buildings remaining from that era.

### Civil War Quests

[Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")

- **[Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks")**: Prove yourself worthy of being a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebel.
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ### Other Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[Rare Gifts](/wiki/Skyrim:Rare_Gifts "Skyrim:Rare Gifts")**: Do a favor by finding a rare item. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

### Courtyard

The Palace is the furthest building from the main gate to Windhelm, along the Valunstrad or "Avenue of Valor". Two guards patrol the courtyard, walking around the two braziers near the building. Another brazier is near the entrance to the courtyard, and the beggar [Silda the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Silda_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Silda the Unseen") often stands here trying to warm herself. There are two doors that both lead to the [Palace of the Kings](#Palace_of_the_Kings). There are two side entrances to the courtyard, one to the west which leads to the residential part of the Stone Quarter, and the other to the east which leads to the more opulent homes above the Gray Quarter.

There is some rubble lying in the courtyard, but there are no signs of damage to the surrounding buildings, and there are two plaques on either side of the entrance, one to Harald and one to Olaf One-Eye, both former rulers of Windhelm. Another plaque to Wulfarth of Atmora can be found outside Candlehearth Hall.

Commemorative Plaques of the Ancient Kings

| [Harald](/wiki/Lore:Harald "Lore:Harald") | [Olaf One-Eye](/wiki/Lore:Olaf_One-Eye "Lore:Olaf One-Eye") | [Wulfharth of Atmora](/wiki/Lore:Wulfharth "Lore:Wulfharth") |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [SR-misc-Harald Plaque.png](/wiki/File:SR-misc-Harald_Plaque.png) | [SR-misc-Olaf Plaque.png](/wiki/File:SR-misc-Olaf_Plaque.png) | [SR-misc-Wulfharth Plaque.png](/wiki/File:SR-misc-Wulfharth_Plaque.png) |
| **HARALD** REIGNED 1E 143 - 221  *13th in the line of Ysgramor and*  *founder of the great Kingdom of*  *Skyrim, where he established fair*  *Windhelm as his capital.* | **OLAF ONE-EYE** REIGNED 1E 420 - 452  *Subdued the foul dragon Numinex,*  *reunited Skyrim after the war of*  *Succession, and conquered the*  *barbarous Reach.* | **WULFHARTH**  **OF ATMORA** REIGNED 1E 480 - 533  *Ysmir, Shor's Tongue, Dragon of the*  *North and noble champion who*  *defeated the Direnni and cleaned*  *Skyrim of the Alessian heresy.* |

#### Main Hall

The main hall of the palace

The Main Hall runs the length of palace. It has two main features, a long table, and a throne carved from a large piece of stone. Either side of the entrance are the doors to the [upper level](#POTKU2) and the [barracks](#Windhelm_Barracks), and at opposite end of the hall are the [war room](#War_Room) and the [kitchen](#Kitchen). Through the war room is another door to a separate section of the [upper level](#Palace_of_the_Kings_Upstairs) of the palace.

The throne, set on a plinth, has a weapon plaque carved above it, two swords behind a shield with the Bear of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") on it. All this has been carved from one large piece of stone, and two small braziers have been set on it to provide some light. On the table, among the food, there is a potion of healing and a potion of stamina.

#### War Room

The War Room is to the west of the throne. The centerpiece of the room is a table with a [map](/wiki/File:SR-item-Civil_War_Map.jpg "File:SR-item-Civil War Map.jpg") marking important tactical locations for the ongoing [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"). There is an iron sword on the table, and on a long table to the south is an assortment of weapons and armor, including a [Stormcloak cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Cuirass "Skyrim:Stormcloak Cuirass"). To the north is the entrance to the Upstairs with the jarl's bedroom.

#### Kitchen

The kitchen is to the east of the throne. The cook, [Sifnar Ironkettle](/wiki/Skyrim:Sifnar_Ironkettle "Skyrim:Sifnar Ironkettle"), spends his days here cooking and cleaning. Counterclockwise around the room there is a long table used for food preparation, a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), and spit by the fire opposite the entrance, three sets of shelves, and a bedroll. The bedroll is unowned and you can sleep in it, if it's not being used.

On the table is a bottle of Alto Wine, two pieces of bread, three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") buds, a gourd, two green apples, a leek, a leg of goat, a mammoth snout, two potatoes, two red apples, a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a tomato, and a piece of venison. Hanging above the table are two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), two [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and three [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). On the middle of the three shelves is a large amount of cheese.

### Palace of the Kings Upstairs (Southern Section)

The southern section of the Palace of the Kings Upstairs has five rooms, one of which belongs to the local [court wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Court_Wizard "Skyrim:Court Wizard"), [Wuunferth the Unliving](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuunferth_the_Unliving "Skyrim:Wuunferth the Unliving"). There are usually two guards patrolling the small corridors, which split to two rooms on either side, and a fifth (Wuunferth's) at the end.

The first room on the left is a dining room. There is a rectangular table with four chairs in the middle of the room, a small round table with two chairs to one side, and a fireplace on the other. There is a cupboard to the left of the door, and a cupboard and a bench on the other side of the room. The cupboard by the door holds a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Knights of the Nine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Knights_of_the_Nine "Skyrim:The Knights of the Nine")* and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). On the cupboard on the other side of the room are copies of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* (a quest starter book), *[2920, First Seed, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_First_Seed,_v3 "Skyrim:2920, First Seed, v3")*, and *[Argonian Account, Book 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Account,_Book_1 "Skyrim:Argonian Account, Book 1")*.

The other three rooms are basic bedrooms with very little decoration or items in them. The second room is a communal bedroom, with four beds, a wardrobe, a dresser, and an end table. The beds are set apart with two back-to-back. The first room on the right has two beds, set apart from each other, and a wardrobe. The second room on the right has two beds, two end tables, and a small table with two chairs. There is a coin purse on the table, and an iron dagger on the long end table by the far wall.

The last room belongs to Wuunferth. There is a trove of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and potions in the room. The main feature of the room is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"). Around the room, clockwise from the door, is an end table, a bed, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), three round tables, a set of shelves, a table, and another set of shelves. On the three round tables there are two [giant's toes](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade"), a [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), two [butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing"), a [luna moth wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing"), two [blue butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"), a [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), and a [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"). On the shelves beside the door are three potions—a [conjurer's philter](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer%27s_Philter "Skyrim:Conjurer's Philter"), a [conjurer's draught](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer%27s_Draught "Skyrim:Conjurer's Draught"), and a [philter of Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Destruction "Skyrim:Philter of Destruction")—three bowls of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), two bowls of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm") and [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), and one bowl each of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), vampire dust, [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), and [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"). On the table is an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem"), a [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), a [solution of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Solution of Lasting Potency"), a [draught of Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Destruction "Skyrim:Draught of Destruction"), a [scroll of blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), and a [scroll of harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"). Finally, on the other set of shelves is another solution of lasting potency.

### Palace of the Kings Upstairs (Northern Section)

The Jarl's bedroom

The northern section of the Palace of the Kings Upstairs has five bedrooms, with the main one belonging to the Jarl. The first four bedrooms each contain a double bed and some sparse furniture, while the fifth, the Jarl's, is far more opulent, with better lighting and a more dynamic design. Two guards patrol the small corridors.

The first room on the left contains a bed, a wardrobe, two end tables, and two chairs. The second room on the left contains a bed, two end tables, a set of shelves, and a table with two chairs. The first room on the right contains a bed, a wardrobe, two end tables, and a table with two chairs. This bed is not owned and can be used by anyone. The second room on the right is used by [Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsarald_Thrice-Pierced "Skyrim:Yrsarald Thrice-Pierced"); it contains a bed, a wardrobe, and three end tables.

The final room belongs to the Jarl. It is larger and more finely decorated than any of the others. The Jarl's bed sits atop a raised wooden platform in the middle of the room, above which there is an extended roof allowing for more windows, and therefore more light, to get into the room. There is also an adept-locked chest at the foot of the bed. Counter-clockwise around the room, there is a wardrobe, a table (with a salt pile and a bowl of bone meal), then an empty chest, some shelves, and finally a table with two chairs. Among the books on the shelves is a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* (which is a quest starter), and on the table by the door is a potion of minor healing.

### Windhelm Barracks

The barracks

The barracks, also known as the **Bloodworks**, are the off-duty and resting area for the guards of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), as well as the location of Windhelm's jail. The entrance to the barracks is to the right, inside the palace. The first room is the guard barracks. There are four beds, three tables with two chairs each, three sets of shelves, a wardrobe, and the prisoner and evidence chest.

The four beds are along the right-hand wall, while the tables are to the left-hand side of the room. There is a sweetroll on the first table, a set of iron gauntlets on the second one, and a couple of books on the last one. There is an iron dagger on the first set of shelves, banded iron armor on the second, and three books on the third set.

The well-lit corridor to the south leads around and down to the jail cells. There are four locked cells in the jail, and in running order they have a master lock, an expert lock, another expert lock, and an adept lock. One of the barrels in the corner contains a bottle of [lotus extract](/wiki/Skyrim:Lotus_Extract "Skyrim:Lotus Extract"). There is nothing else of interest in the jail.

## Notes

- A copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill book *[The Mirror](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mirror "Skyrim:The Mirror")* spawns on the table with the bone meal in the Jarl's bedroom when Captain Aldis's version of Rare Gifts is started.
- If you sided with the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") during the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") questline, most of the displaced Jarls, along with certain members of their courts, will move to the main hall of the palace.
- If you complete the Civil War for the Empire by killing Ulfric and retaking Windhelm for the Legion, guard patrols in the Palace will become comparatively lax - there will no longer be guard patrols in the upstairs rooms, for example. The same is true for [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") should you side with the Stormcloaks.

## Bugs

- The banners near the throne have placement issues such that they clip into the wall behind the throne and the throne itself. These issues exist in an unmodified game and are actually made worse by the [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch").
  -  The clipping is completely resolved by the mod [Banner Clipping Fix for Windhelm Palace of the Kings](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim_Mod:Banner_Clipping_Fix_for_Windhelm_Palace_of_the_Kings&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim Mod:Banner Clipping Fix for Windhelm Palace of the Kings (page does not exist)").
- Guards may not be present upstairs.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- The interior load doors here incorrectly generate wood sounds instead of metal sounds.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- Two books in the Jarl's Quarters may be seen embedded in Ulfric's desk and clipping with each other.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- After completing Battle for Windhelm, the Stormcloak banners don't change for the Imperial one. **?**
