Pale Imperial Camp

**Pale Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), located west of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and northwest of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").

The camp is normally commanded by [Legate Constantius Tituleius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Constantius_Tituleius "Skyrim:Legate Constantius Tituleius"), except during the related quests, at which point [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") will assume command.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Legate Constantius Tituleius](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Constantius_Tituleius "Skyrim:Legate Constantius Tituleius") (commander)  [Imperial Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster")  [Imperial Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier")  [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quests.

## Related Quests

- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)")**: Find and deliver some forged [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents") to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
- **[The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)")**: Take [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Pale Imperial Camp

It is a typical Imperial camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. There is a quartermaster's tent, with a long wooden table out front with various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") on top of the table and inside the tent. Next to this is the workstation for the [Imperial quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster"), consisting of a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). North of the campfire is a row of three small tents containing unowned bed rolls. East of the campfire is the command tent, containing an end table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of their time. Next to the command tent is the Legate's tent, containing an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and an end table beside it. To the right of the tent is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). South of the campfire is the hospital tent, which contains three bed rolls occupied by two wounded soldiers and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Just outside the tent, on the right is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and to the left are some [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") leaning against them. To the right of this tent are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing.

Any time [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") is controlled by the Imperials, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Notes

- There is a [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") vein northeast of the camp.

Pale Stormcloak Camp

**Pale Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), located southeast of [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave") on the south shore of [Lake Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Yorgrim "Skyrim:Lake Yorgrim").

This camp will only be present if the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") hold [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and the rest of the Pale, whether through martial might or via the negotiation during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending"). [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") are camped here under the command of [Frorkmar Banner-Torn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frorkmar_Banner-Torn "Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn"), except during the related quest, when [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") takes command. Like similar military camps that only exist when the hold has changed hands, it has no [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Frorkmar Banner-Torn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frorkmar_Banner-Torn "Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn") (commander)  [Stormcloak Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster")  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier")  [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)")**: Reclaim [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Pale Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. Around the campfire are three small tents containing unowned hay piles. Northwest of the campfire is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table. To the left of the commander's tent is the quartermaster's tent and the workstation for the [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster"), consisting of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). A long wooden table in front of the quartermaster's tent and the tent itself hold various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). To the right of the commander's tent is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). North of the campfire is the command tent, containing a lit brazier, a round table, and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of their time. Northeast of the campfire is the hospital tent, which contains three hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). To the left of the hospital tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). To the right of the hospital tent are some barrels. Northwest of the command tent on the shore of the lake is a [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay_Deposit "Skyrim:Clay Deposit")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") and an [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") vein, while to the east-southeast is a second iron ore vein.

Any time [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Notes

- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map only displays the camp's location; the previous one displayed the camp as well.

## Bugs

- The quartermaster may be missing or tagged as a normal soldier, even though he spends his time using the workstation. **?**

# Skyrim:Pantea's Flute

## Overview

This article is about the quest. For the item, see [Pantea's Flute (item)](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)").

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Find a missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") for [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia").** | |

| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") | | |

Pantea's Flute

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia") at the Bards College.
2. Travel to [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave") and find her missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)").
3. Return to Pantea for your reward.

### Talking to Pantea

When the Fire Festival marks the end of the [Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames") quest, talking to Pantea will bring up the topic of a flute: *"That damn fool! I should ring*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *her neck!"* When asked to elaborate she will explain about a foolish student, [Larina](/wiki/Skyrim:Larina "Skyrim:Larina"), who stole [Pantea's flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") and sold it to a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer"), who believed in Larina's story about the flute being able to make the dead dance. Pantea is understandably upset as the flute has been passed down through seventeen generations, so she asks you to retrieve it for her – right away.

### Hob's Fall Cave

A map marker will now point you towards [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave"), a necromancer den northeast of [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse") in the [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") region. While the cave itself seems straightforward, it has quite a few secrets worth exploring, so enter and take a look around. The ledge overlooking the first room is where you will return after a successful trek, so locate the icy path to the left and make your way through the tunnels and fight the hostile necromancers guarding the desk with a [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a treasure chest. Proceed forward until you reach a suspension bridge. Look over the edge and notice the necromancer camp deep down below, with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and several bedrolls. Use the ledges to jump down for a surprise attack, then loot the camp for a rare [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") and a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill book *[The Exodus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Exodus "Skyrim:The Exodus")*.

### Finding the Flute

Head back up, using the path to get back on track, and then fight the necromancers guarding the next room. Examine the [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") for a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Enchanter's Primer](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanter%27s_Primer "Skyrim:Enchanter's Primer")*, then activate the pull chain and either dodge or destroy the [spellcaster traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap"). The final room is guarded by three necromancers and contains the chest with the flute, a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), and a locked cage containing a dead body. After taking the flute, jump down from the ledge and exit the cave the way you came in.

Back in the Bards College, Pantea will be overwhelmed with joy and will teach you a few tricks she learned while playing for the Winterhold wizards, specifically a one-point boost to all your [Magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Overview "Skyrim:Magic Overview") skills, including [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting"), [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion"), and [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration").

## Notes

- [Isabelle Rolaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine")'s corpse is found at the entrance of the cave if you have started the quest [Drowned Sorrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Drowned_Sorrows "Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows").
- Hob's Fall Cave might be selected as the location for the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold") from the quest [Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)"). If this is the case, then it will be in the same chest as the flute.

## Bugs

- The flute can be found before the quest is given, meaning the marker to turn the quest in never appears, nor will Pantea even offer the quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  -  PC players can use this console command to advance the quest: `setstage bardscollegeflute 40`
- After you turn in the quest, the flute will remain in your inventory, still marked as a quest item.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
  -  PC players can remove the quest item using the following console code: `Player.removeitem 000DABA7 1`
- It's possible that you can turn in the flute to Pantea but the quest won't complete.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Pantea's Flute (BardsCollegeFlute) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Find Pantea's Flute |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Return Pantea's Flute |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 15.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage BardsCollegeFlute stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest BardsCollegeFlute`.

# Skyrim:Pavo's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Pavo's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pavo%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| KolskeggrMinePavosHouse, KolskeggrMineExterior02 | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Northeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Pavo's House

**Pavo's House** is the only house connected to [Kolskeggr Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine"), a [gold mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore") east-northeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

It is the home of local miners [Pavo Attius](/wiki/Skyrim:Pavo_Attius "Skyrim:Pavo Attius") and [Gat gro-Shargakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gat_gro-Shargakh "Skyrim:Gat gro-Shargakh"). It consists of one area only, [Pavo's House](#Pavo.27s_House).

Due to an attack by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), the inhabitants were forced to flee their home and take refuge in the neighboring [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine"). They will move back to the house and Kolskeggr Mine when the quest of the [same name](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolskeggr_Mine_(quest) "Skyrim:Kolskeggr Mine (quest)") is completed.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Gat gro-Shargakh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gat_gro-Shargakh "Skyrim:Gat gro-Shargakh")  [Pavo Attius](/wiki/Skyrim:Pavo_Attius "Skyrim:Pavo Attius") |

## Pavo's House

The Basement

The house consists of a ground floor which is mostly empty and a basement where Pavo and Gat sleep when not working in the mine. The front door opens to the sight of a huge crate on the table with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on top. Another pickaxe is leaning against the eastern wall, next to two food barrels. A [broom](/wiki/Skyrim:Broom "Skyrim:Broom") stands in the southeastern corner. Otherwise, the room is completely empty.

The basement is clearly where the inhabitants spend their time, as it is clean and more furnished than the empty room upstairs. At the foot of the stairs is a food barrel and, hanging above, two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"). Next to the barrel is a set of shelves with plenty of food, including four loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") and an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"). Also on display are two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and three heads of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Adjacent to the shelves stands a small table with a single bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") while a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") is ready in the corner. Two beds stand along the eastern wall, separated by a huge wardrobe with various [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). None of the items in the house are unowned and free to take; the beds are owned by the [Pavo](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions_K#KolskeggrPavoFaction "Skyrim:Factions K") and [Gat](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions_K#KolskeggrGatFaction "Skyrim:Factions K") factions (making them unusable).

# Skyrim:Pawned Prawn

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

The Pawned Prawn

The **Pawned Prawn** is a general goods store in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). The store is owned and run by [Bersi Honey-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand"), although his wife [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa") will take over running the store if anything happens to Bersi. It is located next door to [Black-Briar Meadery](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Meadery "Skyrim:Black-Briar Meadery"), to the west of [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb") near the center of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bersi Honey-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods")  [Drifa](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods") \* |

\* This person only becomes shopkeeper if Bersi is dead.

## Related Quests

- **[Nordic Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry_(quest) "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Jewelry "Skyrim:Nordic Jewelry"): Learn about Nordic jewelry.
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

### Pawned Prawn

The main shop

Upon entering the shop, you will find that the room is also their main living room, where they cook and dine. There is a fireplace opposite the door on the west wall, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front of it. Against the south wall is a cupboard holding [displayed merchandise](#Displayed_Merchandise), including some [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), and to the left is a round wooden table holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and two chairs.

The counter is L-shaped and comes out from the north wall, and holds various displayed merchandise, including a couple [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). Also on the counter are three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Apology "Skyrim:An Apology") from [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm") in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), who refuses to go into [Shroud Hearth Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow "Skyrim:Shroud Hearth Barrow"). This note is here regardless of whether you have cleared the barrow or not.

There is a set of shelves in front of the counter against the north wall that holds only display merchandise and clutter. To the right, against the west wall is a dresser with a Dwarven Urn on top that can be used as a bargaining piece when trying to complete the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business").

Behind the counter, against the west wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, with a wall shelf above holding displayed merchandise, with two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") between the fireplace and chest. Above the counter is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, three bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), all hanging from the ceiling.

### Cellar

There is a door to the north that leads to the residential area. Beyond the door are three [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, with a fourth over a flight of stairs leading down to the cellar. Under the stairs is a pile of firewood and a couple straw bales, with a dresser to the left, against the west wall, holding a bottle of wine. Another food barrel is in the southwestern corner, with a set of shelves to the left, against the south wall. The shelves hold five [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a couple loaves of bread, and several pieces of cheese, with an adept-locked [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") to the left. The safe contains minor loot, plus several copies of a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:To_A_Concerned_Citizen "Skyrim:To A Concerned Citizen") that doesn't seem to have been used in a quest. Beside the safe is a doorway to the south that leads into [Bersi's](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand") and [Drifa's](/wiki/Skyrim:Drifa "Skyrim:Drifa") bedroom. It contains a double bed coming out of the middle of the south wall, with an end table to the left which holds the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), and a wall shelf above holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). At the foot of the bed is a dresser with an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") on top. A chair is against the north wall, and a wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") is in the northwestern corner.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. These items [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Respawning "Skyrim:Dungeons") after ten days.

- Animal Hides: 1 [Leather Strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips")
- Armor: 1 [Iron Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet")
- Arrows: 2 [Iron Arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow")
- Clutter: 1 [Tankard](/wiki/Skyrim:Tankard "Skyrim:Tankard")
- Food: 2 Alto Wine, 3 Bread, 1 [Eidar Cheese Wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), 2 [Eidar Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), 3 [Goat Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), 2 [Green Apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), 2 [Nord Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), 4 Potato, 1 [Red Apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), 1 [Sliced Eidar Cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), 1 Wine
- Ore/Ingots: 2 Iron Ingots
- Potions: 2 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire")
- Weapons: 2 [Iron Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), 1 Iron Sword

These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

# Skyrim:Payment Delivery

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Tell [Thane Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") that the late shipment from [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine") will be arriving soon.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur") |
| Location(s): | [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills"), [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") |
| Reward: | Gold |
| ID: | FreeformStonehillsA |

*"Buy us some time and keep her off our backs."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur") and agree to deliver his message to Bryling.
2. Speak to [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling") about the late shipment and receive a reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Go to [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") and speak to [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur") inside [Sorli's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli%27s_House "Skyrim:Sorli's House"). Ask him if he owns the mine, then continue the conversation until he asks you to take a message to [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling"). It doesn't matter what choices you make in the preceding conversation, all of them lead to Pactur asking to deliver the message:

:   **Do you own the mine?**
:   *"No, and before you ask, it's not for sale."*
:   **I wasn't asking.**
:   *"I'm just protecting Bryling's investment. She's the owner, even though we're the ones here doing all the work. She's already come down hard on us for missing shipments. Likely to do it again, since we're late."*
:   **Do you get many offers?**
:   *"Well, no. But that's not the point. Bryling owns the mine, and she's not selling. We make her some decent coin running this place. Keeps her living well in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). At least, when we can get shipments to her. We're late on the last one. I expect her to start breathin' fire any moment now."*
:   **Is there any way I can help?**
:   *"You could take word to her that there'll be a shipment soon. Buy us some time and keep her off our backs. In exchange, I'm willing to let a few ingots go missing. Maybe more than a few."*
:   **I'll go see Bryling for you.**
:   *"You're doing me quite a favor. I won't forget it. I'm sure she'll be angry. Brace yourself."*

Go to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and find Thane Bryling, either at the Blue Palace by day, or at [her house](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") nearby at night. Tell her you have a message from Pactur. After informing her that the shipment will arrive soon, Bryling will reward you with a small amount of gold:

:   **Pactur asked me to deliver a message.**
:   *"Is everything all right? I've not heard from [Sorli](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") or Pactur in some time."*
:   **Everything is fine. The shipment will be here soon.**
:   *"That's good news. I was starting to fear something had happened.
    You have my thanks."*

## Notes

- Despite Pactur mentioning he will let you take [ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingots "Skyrim:Ingots") as a reward for delivering the message to Bryling, you can already take the ingots around the smelter without penalty.
- With either [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") or the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") installed, Pactur will move to Morthal if Sorli takes over as Jarl.

## Quest Stages

| Payment Delivery (FreeformStonehillsA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Speak with Bryling |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformStonehillsA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformStonehillsA`.

# Skyrim:Peak's Shade Tower

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |

| East of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") Southwest of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch") | |

Peak's Shade Tower

**Peak's Shade Tower** is a small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan").

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

Following the main road east out of Falkreath toward [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), the path leading up to the tower is marked by a cairn on the right side of the road. Three [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), one [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and a patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") fungus on a large tree stump are found just outside the entrance.

The tower has long eroded, and the only inhabitant is a spriggan. The interior is overgrown with vegetation, including two [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), one purple mountain flower, and two [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"). It is also a good place to find [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") and [monarch butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Monarch_Butterfly "Skyrim:Monarch Butterfly") during the day, and a few [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth") or [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") at night. Hidden among the vegetation along the west wall of the tower is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

## Notes

- With *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* installed, the spriggan may be an Earth Mother, depending on what level you approach the ruin.

# Skyrim:Pelagia Farm

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Pelagia Farm

**Pelagia Farm** is a large farm south of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") owned by [Severio Pelagia](/wiki/Skyrim:Severio_Pelagia "Skyrim:Severio Pelagia").

It is a sprawling farm, with a small single-story building maintained by [Nimriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimriel "Skyrim:Nimriel") and [Gloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloth "Skyrim:Gloth"). They live at the farm, while Severio lives in his [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Severio_Pelagia%27s_House "Skyrim:Severio Pelagia's House") in Whiterun.

When approaching Pelagia Farm for the first time, you will come across [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress"), [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas"), and [Ria](/wiki/Skyrim:Ria "Skyrim:Ria") battling a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"). The group of [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") will always win the fight.

## Residents

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | Residents | | --- | | **[Gloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloth "Skyrim:Gloth")**  **[Nimriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimriel "Skyrim:Nimriel")** | |

## Related Quests

- **[Gather Wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Gather_Wheat "Skyrim:Gather Wheat")**: Get paid to gather crops. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Speak with the leader of the Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Speak_with_the_leader_of_the_Companions "Skyrim:Speak with the leader of the Companions")**: Prove you are worthy to join the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").

### Exterior

There are at least three fields of [vegetables](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Fruit.2FVegetables "Skyrim:Food") with either stone walls or fences segregating them. During the day, [Severio Pelagia](/wiki/Skyrim:Severio_Pelagia "Skyrim:Severio Pelagia") is in the fields with his workers. He will gladly buy any [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") or [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") you hold. There is a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling") to the east of the house and several other outbuildings and storage sheds around the property. To the west of the house is a pen for a [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") and a few paces in front of the entrance are a couple of [chickens' nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg").

| Crops | Plants | Mushrooms | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 30 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")  12 [Leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek")  12 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") | 1 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender")  2 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 1 [Mora Tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") | 2 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken")  1 [Cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Pelagia Farm

Farmstead interior

Upon entering there is a long wooden table and bench on your left against the west wall, with an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a few [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), three [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") containing several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on the table, with a chair at either end and a wall shelf above holding crockery. On your right as you enter, against the east wall are a stack of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and sacks next to a bookcase holding fourteen common books, a copy of *[Songs of Skyrim: Revised](/wiki/Skyrim:Songs_of_Skyrim:_Revised "Skyrim:Songs of Skyrim: Revised")* and a bowl containing a cabbage. Next to this is a doorway to a bedroom. In the northwest corner of the room is a cupboard holding a cabbage, a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), among piles of crockery. There is a chair next to the cupboard with a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and a couple of [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") on the floor and two more wall shelves above holding clutter. There is a second doorway on the east wall with a large fire pit between the two of them with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it.

The first bedroom contains a single bed against the north wall and a dresser beside it with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") in a bowl, and a copy of *[Rising Threat, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_Threat,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Rising Threat, Vol. IV")* on top. There is a chair in the southeastern corner. The second bedroom contains a single bed against the south wall, with an end table beside it, holding a bottle of ale, a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), and copies of *[Yngol and the Sea-Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_and_the_Sea-Ghosts "Skyrim:Yngol and the Sea-Ghosts")* and *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*. A narrow table against the north wall holds a bottle of ale, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on a plate, two common books, and a [draught of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health"). Underneath it is a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots").

## Notes

- Though you can find and activate a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling") here, it will only lead to an animation, with no actual function in the game even with *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* installed.
- Even if you help Severio Pelagia, everything in the farmhouse may still be considered owned, and entering may still count as trespassing.
-  Version 2.1.1 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the barrels outside the building as owned by the farm.

# Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Penitus Oculatus Outpost

The **Penitus Oculatus Outpost** is the headquarters of the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") order in Skyrim, located in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge").

It consists of one zone, *[Penitus Oculatus Outpost](#Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!")**: Finish the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") and rid Skyrim of their kind.

## Exterior

| Plants | Other |
| --- | --- |
| 1 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") | 1 [Tanning Rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning")  1 [Workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") |

## Penitus Oculatus Outpost

Penitus Oculatus Outpost interior

Immediately to the left upon entering is a respawning food barrel next to a table holding four loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), four bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), four pieces of [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), one [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). Above the table are several hanging ingredients, including three portions of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), four portions of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids. To the right of the table is a woven basket containing eight [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and a respawning meat barrel with one [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and two [potions of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") resting atop it. Above the basket and barrel are two hanging racks, one of which holds three freshly caught [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") while the other holds two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and another rabbit.

In the northwest corner is a single bed with a small non-respawning chest at its foot. A basket containing three [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") sits on the floor to the right of the bed, along with another respawning food barrel holding three bottles of Nord mead on top. Another single bed with a small non-respawning chest at its foot is situated next to this food barrel, and a copy of the book *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")* is stashed beneath the bed. Next to this bed, directly across from the front door, is the fireplace, where four bottles of Nord mead and one bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") are found on the mantel. The base of the fireplace holds a kettle containing five [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast") on the left, and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") on the right. In front of the fireplace is a small table holding an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), five loose gold coins, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and three bottles of Nord mead. To the right of the fireplace is a non-respawning end table. A small non-respawning chest rests on the floor at the center of the east wall, flanked by a single bed on each side.

## Notes

- The porch of the outpost hosts five respawning food barrels, a respawning sack, a workbench, a tanning rack, and a table holding a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and a copy of a random common book, such as *[Palla, volume 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Palla,_volume_1 "Skyrim:Palla, volume 1")* or *[2920, Sun's Dawn, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Sun%27s_Dawn,_v2 "Skyrim:2920, Sun's Dawn, v2")*.
- All four beds here belong to the [PenitusOculatusFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:PenitusOculatusFaction "Skyrim:PenitusOculatusFaction").
- Dialogue between [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") and a Penitus Oculatus Agent during the quest [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") indicates that the outpost is supposed to be abandoned once the Emperor leaves Skyrim, though this never occurs in-game. (See [below](#Bugs) for a workaround)

## Bugs

- If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capture Solitude, this outpost will remain active in Dragon Bridge, which can result in Penitus Oculatus agents and [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") engaging each other in combat.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. If [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") questline and the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") questline for the Stormcloaks are finished, the outpost will be cleared out.

# Skyrim:People

## Overview

This page serves as a listing of all the **named NPCs** in the game. It does not include generic enemies such as bandits. Some NPCs can become [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), who will travel with you and fight for you.

[‡](#note_Ghorza)Ghorza gra-Bagol only offers services at the forge located outside the Castle Markarth proper (just north of The Hag's Cure).

[^a](#note_dieToD)These people can die as part of the [Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death") quest.

[^b](#note_dieFC)These people can die as part of the [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") quest.

[^c](#note_dieNOECM)These people can die as part of the [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") quest.

[^d](#note_dieEnter)These people can die when you first enter the city.

[^e](#note_dieHoH)Vigilant Tyranus can die as part of the [House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors") quest.

[^f](#note_Banning)Banning is not a potential follower, but will sell the canine follower Vigilance.

[^g](#note_Fjotra)Fjotra only appears after the quest [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella").

[^d](#note_ship)Provides initial transportation to [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim").

[^e](#note_ferry)This [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Transport#FerrymenDG "Skyrim:Transport") can be hired to transport you between cities via boat.

[^f](#note_j.27datharr)Appears during [Find the Thalmor Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_the_Thalmor_Assassin "Skyrim:Find the Thalmor Assassin").

### Winterhold People

    | --- | --- |
    | [^](#note_Unbound) |  |

    These people are only in Helgen during the opening quest, [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), and upon completion will relocate elsewhere in Skyrim.
:   b.

    |  |  |
    | --- | --- |
    | [^](#note_Dead) |  |

    These people are killed during [Alduin](/wiki/Skyrim:Alduin "Skyrim:Alduin")'s attack on Helgen.
:   c.

    |  |  |
    | --- | --- |
    | [^](#note_Lokir) |  |

    [Lokir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lokir "Skyrim:Lokir") is killed during the opening cutscene while attempting to escape the Imperial Legion.

### Thirsk People DB

Residents are only present at this location if you complete the quest [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") in the Nords' favor. Before this point, they will be found at [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat") or elsewhere as noted.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| | [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") | | --- | | **[Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy")** ‡ **[Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus")** † **[Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur")** [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")‡ **[Herkja](/wiki/Skyrim:Herkja "Skyrim:Herkja")** § **[Hilund](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilund "Skyrim:Hilund")** ‡ **[Kuvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kuvar "Skyrim:Kuvar")** [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Heavy Armor (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Heavy Armor (Master)")‡ **[Sirkjorg](/wiki/Skyrim:Sirkjorg "Skyrim:Sirkjorg")** § | |

‡ Found at the [Beast Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Stone "Skyrim:Beast Stone") at night after you witness the dialogue between Bujold the Unworthy and Kuvar at Bujold's Retreat and until the stone has been cleansed during the quest [Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones").

### World Encounters

The following NPCs are part of [random encounters](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") and wander randomly:

- **[Afflicted Refugee](/wiki/Skyrim:Afflicted_Refugee "Skyrim:Afflicted Refugee")**
- **[Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen")**
- **[Balbus](/wiki/Skyrim:Balbus "Skyrim:Balbus")**
- **[Bottar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bottar "Skyrim:Bottar")** and **[Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(child) "Skyrim:Sond (child)")**
- **[Dawnguard Novice Hakar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Novice_Hakar "Skyrim:Dawnguard Novice Hakar")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")
- **[Deep-In-His-Cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep-In-His-Cups "Skyrim:Deep-In-His-Cups")**
- **[Faldrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldrus "Skyrim:Faldrus")**
- **[M'aiq the Liar](/wiki/Skyrim:M%27aiq_the_Liar "Skyrim:M'aiq the Liar")**
- **[Old Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Orc "Skyrim:Old Orc")**
- **[Plautis Carvain](/wiki/Skyrim:Plautis_Carvain "Skyrim:Plautis Carvain")**
- **[Salonia Carvain](/wiki/Skyrim:Salonia_Carvain "Skyrim:Salonia Carvain")**
- **[Sigar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigar "Skyrim:Sigar")**
- **[Talsgar the Wanderer](/wiki/Skyrim:Talsgar_the_Wanderer "Skyrim:Talsgar the Wanderer")**
- **[Taron Dreth](/wiki/Skyrim:Taron_Dreth "Skyrim:Taron Dreth")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")

# Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Dillonn241](/wiki/User:Dillonn241 "User:Dillonn241"), checked by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless") |

| ID: | ccVSVSSE002\_MainQuest |
| Added by: | [Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim") |

A farmhand's journal reveals a multitude of animals waiting to be rescued

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read the [*For Sale*](/wiki/Skyrim:For_Sale "Skyrim:For Sale") notice at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare").
2. Purchase a goat in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") for 200 gold and read [*Halvar's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Halvar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Halvar's Journal").
3. Locate the tame fox south of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill") and feed it a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll").
4. Locate the rabbit at the [Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack") and feed it a [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot").
5. Kill the [Vampire Naturalist](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Naturalist "Skyrim:Vampire Naturalist") in [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave") and rescue the tame spider.
6. Find the tame skeever within [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Skeever Cage Key") to unlock its cage.

## Detailed Walkthrough

A trained goat is for sale in Whiterun Hold

### Goat for Sale

In [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), a [*For Sale*](/wiki/Skyrim:For_Sale "Skyrim:For Sale") notice can be found at the counter. It is advertising for the sale of [Hilda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilda "Skyrim:Hilda"), a trained pack [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").

Journey to Rorikstead and locate [Halvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Halvar "Skyrim:Halvar") in order to purchase the goat. Halvar is a farmhand who can be found working the field beside [Cowflop Farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowflop_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Cowflop Farmhouse"). He will sell Hilda for 200 gold, at which point it will act as your follower and can be given various orders such as instructions to wait at a specified [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities") or [player house](/wiki/Skyrim:Houses "Skyrim:Houses").

Upon purchasing Hilda, you will be prompted to read [*Halvar's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Halvar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Halvar's Journal") to find out more about the goat. It can be found on Halvar's bedroll next to the field. Reading it will reveal that Halvar had come across many other tame animals in his travels, and your journal will update with objectives to track down each of them. They can be found and rescued in any order you wish.

Sweet Roll stands over the body of its former master

### A Bosmer and His Fox

In the forest south-southwest of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill"), you will come across a collared fox named [Sweet Roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll_(creature) "Skyrim:Sweet Roll (creature)") standing over the body of a [Bosmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") [thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(Pets_of_Skyrim) "Skyrim:Thief (Pets of Skyrim)"). If you are having trouble finding it, stand beside the pile of rocks (the cairn) at the north end of the bridge and walk south; cross over the stream on foot; he is located right over the hill at about a total of 37 running steps from the cairn. A detect dead spell will show one blue and two red bodies. The thief was probably killed by [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), as evidenced by the scattered [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow") and the two wolf carcasses surrounding him. His body can be looted for some ill-gotten treasure as well as the [*Thief's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Thief's Journal").

Reading the journal will reveal that the fox has a penchant for [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") (thus the name). It will refuse to interact with you until you have a sweet roll in your inventory, at which point you can feed and tame it. Fortunately, the thief has five sweet rolls on his body.

### Alchemist Bunny

A tame [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") named [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_(creature) "Skyrim:Thistle (creature)") can be found at the abandoned [Alchemist's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Alchemist's Shack") in the mountain pass south of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). The nearby [*Notes on Tamed Rabbit*](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_on_Tamed_Rabbit "Skyrim:Notes on Tamed Rabbit") will reveal that Thistle enjoys [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). A trough of carrots can be found right next to the rabbit, making it a simple matter to feed and tame it.

Some vampires prefer the taste of fear, others the taste of pain

### The Taste of Pain

You will be led to the hidden [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") lair within the spider-infested [Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave") in order to obtain a pet [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") named [Arachnia](/wiki/Skyrim:Arachnia "Skyrim:Arachnia"). It has been tamed by a [Vampire Naturalist](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Naturalist "Skyrim:Vampire Naturalist"), who is using it to harvest vast amounts of venom for the purpose of torturing her victims before she drinks their blood.

Kill the vampire and loot the [Spider Cage Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Spider Cage Key") from her corpse in order to free Arachnia from its cage. You can also loot the [*Vampire Naturalist's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Naturalist%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Vampire Naturalist's Journal") for some background information on her experiments. Once the cage is opened, Arachnia is yours.

Free Skritch from a grisly fate

### A Skooma-Sucker's Dinner

Within [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), you will come across a tame [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") named [Skritch](/wiki/Skyrim:Skritch "Skyrim:Skritch") found locked in a cage. You can find the body of its owner just across from the entrance to [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"): a failed [pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket_(person) "Skyrim:Pickpocket (person)") who planned to catch skeevers for food but decided to train one instead for use as a distraction. Loot the [Skeever Cage Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Cage_Key "Skyrim:Skeever Cage Key") from his corpse and open the cage in order to rescue Skritch and claim the animal as your own. You can also read the [*Pickpocket's Journal*](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Pickpocket's Journal") for optional background information.

### Pets of Skyrim

Once you've obtained the last of the 5 pets, the quest concludes. Like other Creation Club pets, each one can obey a range of orders and each also has its own distinct attribute. Arachnia can place paralysis web traps and provide [Potent Frostbite Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Potent_Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Potent Frostbite Venom"); Hilda can provide [Jugs of Milk](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug_of_Milk "Skyrim:Jug of Milk"); Skritch can locate or provide [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") items; Sweet Roll can locate or provide loot; and Thistle can locate plants which can be harvested for [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). Some of the pets can also be equipped with an [Animal Collar](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Collar "Skyrim:Animal Collar") or an [Animal Pack](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Pack "Skyrim:Animal Pack"), two items added by Pets of Skyrim; indeed, Hilda is already wearing a pack, and Sweet Roll a collar. The collar is simply aesthetic, but the pack provides a real benefit by increasing the pet's carrying capacity by 40.

Each time you get a pet a new "Teleport: <Pet's Name>" spell appears. This can be used to retrieve your lost pet if it ever gets "misplaced".

## Bugs

- The *[For Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:For_Sale "Skyrim:For Sale")* note, *[Halvar's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Halvar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Halvar's Journal")*, the *[Notes on Tamed Rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_on_Tamed_Rabbit "Skyrim:Notes on Tamed Rabbit")*, and the *[Thief's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Thief's Journal")* all remain marked as quest items even after the quest ends, resulting in them being stuck in your inventory permanently.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.318, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed with the console commands `player.dropitem <ID>` or `player.removeitem <ID>` where <ID> is the [ID](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID") of the item you want to drop from your inventory.
- If you purchase the goat from Halvar in Rorikstead before reading the *[For Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:For_Sale "Skyrim:For Sale")* note, the marker directing the player to purchase the goat from Halvar may not be able to be marked as cleared.
- If you do not purchase the goat from Halvar before collecting all the other pets, the quest will still complete and the goat will be unobtainable -- although the dialogue option to buy it will remain there, it will have no effect besides making you lose 200 gold. **?**

I should set out to find them. *Objective :* Find the tamed rabbit  *Objective :* Find the tamed skeever  *Objective :* Find the tamed spider  *Objective :* Find the tamed fox |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 20, 120, 220, 320, 420, 520.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccVSVSSE002_MainQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccVSVSSE002_MainQuest`.

# Skyrim:Pieces of the Past

## Overview
